League of Nations Begins General Debate, Eden Eloquently Speaks, Explaining British Policy, European Groups Confronting Each Other Threaten Peace, Tolerance and Self-Restraint are Crucial to Maintaining Order, Western Representative Accuses Countries of Interfering with the War's Conduct

(Geneva) British Foreign Secretary Eden addressed the League of Nations Assembly today on Britain's policy in Europe, saying that Britain does not want to see European countries divided into two groups due to their political systems. The seriousness of the current situation warrants a frank speech, so his choice of words today may not be as cautious as usual, and he hopes that the attendees will forgive him.

Nationalism is now very strong, and two different political systems have become confrontational. Trust is weakening everywhere in the world. Countries are now spending an increasing portion of their national wealth on armaments, even though it is detrimental to their economies. This is not a good phenomenon, but it is not yet hopeless. Countries can still work together. They must prioritize tolerance and self-restraint. Disparaging other countries' political systems will not enhance the respect for their own. Britain does not allow anyone to seize its democracy, which is an essential element for everyone striving for freedom, personality, and peace. It should be understood that just as I view my own political system, others have the same view of their own. Britain fully and completely accepts this principle. The first essential for countries to live in order is to believe in their own national ideology while tolerating the ideologies of other countries. Trust in the future is an indispensable factor for economic recovery. They must respect each other's national systems, and they also need an international order. This order should ultimately act as an arbitrator for disputes between countries.

Now, we must find a way to implement this agreement, and only then can civilization be preserved. Otherwise, civilization will perish. The British government's policy is to instill this belief in the League of Nations. When considering the future of the League of Nations, we should focus on two aspects: one is the League's machinery, and the other is the willingness to use this machinery. The latter is much more important than the former, but the machinery also needs to be improved.

The Foreign Secretary then discussed the recent failures of collective security, saying that the main reasons were the lack of universality and the failure to take more forceful intervention in its early stages. Now, only by striving for universality can the League of Nations be given full effect and threats to peace be curbed.

The Foreign Secretary further touched upon plans to improve the League of Nations' covenant, saying that the British government believes that in the early stages of every dispute, the members of the League of Nations Council must clearly indicate what kind of intervention they are prepared to make to preserve peace. This is absolutely essential. The British government believes that regional agreements can find ways to enhance the implementation of the League of Nations' covenant, so the British government is determined to negotiate such agreements with Western European countries. As for the raw materials issue, it should be given due discussion by the League of Nations. Britain is prepared to have the League of Nations Assembly take steps in this direction.

The Foreign Secretary finally discussed the issue of armaments, saying that Britain must wait for countries to conclude an arms limitation treaty before it can cease its current course of action. In fact, disarmament involves not only military matters but also the spirit. Not only should armaments be put down, but the spirit of militarism should also be eliminated. Britain cannot sit idly by while countries arbitrarily expand their armaments to seek to inflate their power. The Foreign Secretary concluded by appealing to the League of Nations Assembly to strive to establish an international mechanism to resolve disputes between countries and avoid resorting to force. (Reuters dispatch on the 25th)

Four Key Points of British Foreign Secretary's Speech

(Geneva) The League of Nations Assembly resumed its meeting at 10:00 AM this morning and began a general debate on political issues. British Foreign Secretary Eden was the first to deliver a speech, advocating for a total of four points: (1) The League of Nations Covenant should be separated from the Treaty of Versailles. (2) International agreements should be concluded to adjust the trade in raw materials. (3) The British government is prepared to cooperate with all countries to establish a general disarmament convention, but "spiritual disarmament" should be implemented at the same time. (4) The British government is prepared to negotiate regional conventions with Western European countries, but these conventions must be integrated with the League of Nations Covenant and approved by the League of Nations Assembly and the Council. In addition, Eden praised the democratic system, saying that it best protects freedom and maintains peace. However, he said that although the British government believes in the democratic system more than other countries, it will not make any sacrifices because of this belief. His conclusion was that if the world's countries are divided into several groups that confront each other, the impact will only make the world's complex situation even more unnecessarily complicated. It is hoped that all countries can be tolerant of each other so that the world can restore order and re-establish normal economic relations, upon which the world's economic recovery truly depends. (Havas dispatch on the 25th)

Western Representative Accuses of Supplying Arms

Confident that the Government Will Be Able to Suppress the Rebellion After Foreign Secretary Eden finished his speech, Spanish Foreign Minister Bardy took the floor, saying that the government of my country can now prove that the non-intervention agreement concluded by various countries because of the civil strife in my country actually benefits the rebels. If my country had not encountered a similar situation, the civil strife would have ended long ago. What is aggression? It is when certain countries supply arms to the rebels. Bardy then put forward the conclusion: the government of my country is confident that it will be able to quell the civil strife. The people of my country, who do not want to live under a dictatorial regime, number in the millions, how can they sit idly by and wait to die? (Havas dispatch on the 25th)

(Geneva) Spanish Foreign Minister Bardy today attacked the policy of non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War in a speech to the League of Nations Assembly, calling it an interventionist policy that is detrimental to the Spanish government. Bardy reserved the right to raise the matter in the League of Nations at a later date. Bardy said that the manner of non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War is a legal oddity, and it is what the political system and the rebels want. The spiritual and material assistance given to the rebels by various countries, in short, the so-called non-intervention is actively interfering on behalf of the rebels in order to blockade the Spanish government. (Reuters dispatch on the 25th)

After the Spanish Foreign Minister finished his speech, the League of Nations Assembly adjourned until tomorrow morning. The Council is scheduled to discuss the issue of the Free City of Danzig at 4:30 PM today. (Havas dispatch on the 25th)

[South American Representatives Discuss the Situation in Spain

(Paris) The correspondent of the Morning Post stationed in Geneva recently stated that the representatives of the South American countries in the League of Nations held a meeting last night to discuss the situation in Spain. The representatives of six countries (there are a total of nine South American member states in the League of Nations) said that their respective governments were prepared to recognize the National Army Government in Burgos City. If Spanish Foreign Minister Bardy made any intemperate remarks in his speech to the Assembly this morning, they would withdraw from the meeting hall and let the Uruguayan representative continue to attend. According to opinions from political circles in Rome, the League of Nations' decision to allow Abyssinia to attend has indeed created a serious situation, but because Italy has not sent a representative to Geneva at the moment, the League of Nations' move will not necessarily force Italy to take action, and it is deeply believed that the League of Nations will eventually recognize that Abyssinia should not have a representative attending one day. The current resolution is only slightly delayed. (Reuters dispatch on the 24th)

(Rome) An Associated Press reporter learned today that Prime Minister Mussolini, after studying the recent situation, has decided to remain in the League of Nations for the time being. There are two reasons for Mussolini's decision: (1) Before the League of Nations prohibits Abyssinian representatives from attending, Italy's refusal to cooperate with the League of Nations is tantamount to withdrawing from the League of Nations in fact. (2) Formal withdrawal would indicate that Italy and Germany are already taking consistent steps, but Mussolini deeply desires that Britain and Italy can reach a compromise on the situation in the Mediterranean. (Paris) According to information obtained by the "Paris Evening News" correspondent in Rome, the Italian government has strictly ordered the Italian military authorities in the Abyssinian capital to quickly occupy all of Abyssinian territory, especially the Goro region where the central government of Abyssinia is located, so that the Abyssinian government will have no place to establish itself, and the international community will have no further excuse for intervention. Our Country Hopeful for a Permanent Council Seat

(Geneva) The First Committee of the League of Nations General Assembly, the Legal and Regulatory Committee, passed a resolution at today's meeting to temporarily increase the original nine non-permanent council seats of the League of Nations Administrative Council to eleven. One of the two additional seats will be retained by Portugal for continuous tenure, and the other seat is specially added for China. In addition, the terms of the original non-permanent council members, Argentina, Australia, and Denmark, have expired this year and will be re-elected by this General Assembly. French Representative Proposes Reopening Disarmament Negotiations; British Government Expresses Willingness to Support; Success Unlikely Without German Participation

(Geneva) The French delegation attending the League of Nations General Assembly has formally notified the General Assembly's Presidium, proposing to reconvene the disarmament conference to discuss the issue of limiting and reducing armaments. The disarmament conference was convened in 1932, but work was suspended in October 1933 due to Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations. Because the arms race among nations is extremely fierce, France has proposed reopening the disarmament conference, and the United Kingdom is also supporting it. However, with Germany and Italy not participating in the work of the League of Nations, it is uncertain whether the disarmament conference can achieve practical results. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

(Geneva) The French Foreign Minister today notified the Presidium of the League of Nations General Assembly, proposing that the League of Nations convene a presidium for the disarmament conference in order to reopen negotiations on arms limitation. France hopes that the solution to various European problems and the ultimate reduction of armaments can be achieved by starting from the economic aspect, which will be smoother than focusing solely on the political aspect. According to the Presidium, it was once advocated that disarmament negotiations could continue based on the following points: (1) control the manufacture and trade of arms; (2) publicize the military expenditure of budget proposals; (3) establish a permanent disarmament committee; (4) guarantee the implementation of all plans negotiated. (Reuters dispatch, 24th)

British Conservative Leader Strongly Advocates British-French Cooperation to Jointly Resist Fascism; Preparedness in Land, Sea, and Air Forces

(Paris) Former Chancellor of the Exchequer and First Lord of the Admiralty, Winston Churchill, leader of the British Conservative opposition, recently came to France and gave a public speech at the "Ambassador Theatre" here this afternoon, advocating that the two democratic countries of Britain and France should strengthen their air force power to jointly resist Fascism, saying, "France has the strongest army in the world, and Britain has the largest navy in the world. Therefore, only when Britain and France live in harmony can world peace be maintained. The policies of the two countries towards Geneva should be realistic and not be bound by principles. Dictatorial countries are now threatening the legacy of democratic politics, so democratic countries must have a way to defend themselves. Only when the French Republic and the British Empire join hands to seek peace and freedom can there be a solution. Moreover, our Britain and France are by no means weak and helpless, as rumored by the outside world. Remembering four years ago, the international situation was still different from today. At that time, I advocated British-French cooperation. Now, I thank God that the French army has become the most superior army in the world. As for the British navy, I dare say that it is far stronger than in 1914. Not only is it stronger than any one country's navy, but even if the navies of all European countries are combined, they are only enough to be enemies with the British navy. Now, the only thing that has become a problem is the air force. Therefore, Britain and France should make greater efforts on this issue to make the democratic countries invincible in the world. However, in any case, it would be a big mistake to think that the air forces of Britain and France currently have no defensive capabilities." (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Warsaw According to a published document here, the Soviet Russian budget had a deficit of 300 million rubles as of September 11. Spanish Government's Water Attack Strategy Succeeds; Counter-Offensive Begins Against Enemy Positions in the Southwest; Floodwaters Rush Like a Thousand Horses; Many Rebels Drown Before They Can Escape

Madrid The Spanish government army yesterday opened the floodgates of the Albacete River on the southern front, releasing 10 million cubic meters of water to stop the rebels from advancing along the Tagus River basin. The capital was extremely jubilant upon learning of the government army's success with this water attack strategy. When the rebels were advancing along the already dried-up riverbed, they did not expect the floodwaters to rush in like a thousand horses, and many drowned before they could escape. It is also learned that one column of the rebel army, led by Colonel Yague, which was advancing towards Toledo, has been cut off by the floodwaters. At the same time, it is learned that the government army's front line has moved forward twenty miles. It is said that the government army will continue to release water until the rebels are completely routed. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Madrid It is learned that the government army has begun a fierce counter-offensive against the rebels on the Talavera and Santolalla front lines southwest of Madrid and is now approaching the Talavera position. This victory of the government army is due to the effect of opening the floodgates of the Albacete River yesterday. After the floodgates were opened, 4 million cubic meters of accumulated water rushed to the plains, and many rebels were submerged. A large amount of food and ammunition were swept away by the floodwaters. The government army column, led by Colonel Navarro, took the opportunity to launch an attack and went straight to Talavera. The rebels had to abandon the positions destroyed by the water. Regarding the detailed battle situation, the government is keeping it strictly secret. In general, the government army's advance has not yet made contact with the rebels. According to a communiqué issued by the Ministry of War, the government army began an offensive on the Talavera front, and the rebels suddenly retreated. On the central front, in the Navarre-Beral region, the government army attacked three positions occupied by foreign troops in the rebel army, seized a large amount of military supplies, and defeated the rebel cavalry. In addition, government aircraft continued to bomb the city of Oviedo, which will soon fall. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Remaining Garrison in Ancient Castle South of the Capital Resists; Rebel Aircraft Supply Food and Ammunition

Seville Radio station of the Nationalist Army broadcasted news that the column led by General Yague had approached the city of Toledo and was about to occupy it. In the rubble of the Alcazar fortress in the city, a part of the young officers and soldiers are still defending it to the death. The Nationalist Army is now dropping food and ammunition by aircraft to replenish them. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Toledo Although the Spanish government claims to have occupied the ancient castle of Alcazar in Toledo, it is learned that the castle is still in the hands of the rebels. The government army has now launched a new attack on the castle, but judging from the situation, the garrison, which has resisted for ten weeks, seems to be able to hold out for at least several more days. At the same time, the rebel high command, after occupying the Makqueda fortress, is now preparing to make a final assault on Toledo. However, the rebel commander, General Franco, believes that it is advisable to proceed cautiously. Although the Spanish Nationalists are eager to rescue their brave comrades in the fortress, everything will be carried out prudently according to military strategy to avoid endangering the entire war. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

German Fabrication; Protest from Romania and Czechoslovakia; Military Plans Are Entirely Fictitious

Japan's Next Year's Huge Budget Exceeds 3 Billion Yen

(Tokyo) Although the Ministry of Finance has made routine reductions to the amounts requested by various ministries for Japan's 1937-38 budget, the total amount will undoubtedly exceed ¥3,000,000,000. The ¥3,204,491,000 budget for the next fiscal year includes ¥1,865,500,000 in basic expenses and ¥1,338,991,000 in supplementary budgets. The new requests submitted by the Army and Navy total ¥826,000,000, accounting for 65% of the supplementary budget. The above figures do not include interest on new bonds projected by the Ministry of Finance, as well as expenses for tax reorganization and various improvements. If these are included, the total budget may increase to ¥3,300,000,000. If the ¥200,000,000 decided by the Ministry of Home Affairs and the Ministry of Finance for local financial reorganization is added, the total budget will increase to ¥3,500,000,000. The Ministry of Finance's desire to reduce the budget by as much as ¥400,000,000 or ¥500,000,000 may not be realized. The draft budgets submitted by the various ministries are as follows:

(1) Basic Budget: Ministry of the Imperial Household ¥4,500,000, Ministry of Foreign Affairs ¥19,300,000, Ministry of Home Affairs ¥144,000, Ministry of Finance ¥461,300,000, Ministry of the Army ¥336,000,000, Ministry of the Navy ¥430,000,000, Ministry of Justice ¥39,000,000, Ministry of Education ¥134,600,000, Ministry of Agriculture ¥75,100,000, Ministry of Commerce ¥13,400,000, Ministry of Communications ¥191,500,000, Ministry of Colonial Affairs ¥16,300,000, Total: ¥1,865,500,000.

(2) Supplementary Budget: Ministry of Foreign Affairs ¥30,000,000, Ministry of Home Affairs ¥121,700,000, Ministry of Finance ¥11,500,000, Ministry of the Army ¥486,000,000, Ministry of the Navy ¥340,000,000, Ministry of Justice ¥6,000,000, Ministry of Education ¥55,687,000, Ministry of Agriculture ¥101,000,000, Ministry of Commerce ¥27,724,000, Ministry of Communications ¥58,000,000, Ministry of Colonial Affairs ¥17,780,000, Total: ¥1,338,991,000. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

French Financial Panic Worsens; Bank Discount Rate Increased to 5%; Franc Devaluation Seems Unlikely to Be Implemented Immediately

(Paris) The Bank of France's interest rate has risen to 5%, which has greatly surprised the public. The bank issued a weekly report today stating that gold reserves have decreased by another 840 million francs. The increase in the discount rate from 3% to 5% has caused a kind of political panic. The government's cheap money policy has long been known, but this measure had to be taken to curb the outflow of gold. Since 1931, the amount of gold outflow has reached a huge 35,000,000,000 francs. The Bank of France's gold reserves currently total 52,691,000,000 francs, which is still more than the statutory reserve amount, but is gradually approaching 50,000,000,000. If it is necessary to prepare for any unexpected events, such as war, this number will be reduced as much as possible. (Reuters dispatch, 24th)

(Paris) Public opinion seems to suggest that the devaluation of the franc will not be decided immediately. It is reported that French Finance Minister Rivol has now drafted a strict procedure to restore the treasury and will submit it to the cabinet meeting this afternoon. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) After the Bank of France's discount rate was raised from 3% to 5%, various newspapers here commented on it. Le Petit Parisien reported, "In the past month, the Bank of France's cash reserves have continued to flow out of the country. This is the direct reason for the bank's increase in the discount rate." Le Petit Journal reported, "The outflow of French cash is abnormal and unreasonable, whether from a financial situation or from French politics. Now that the Bank of France has raised the discount rate by two percentage points, it can be corrected." L'Écho de Paris published an article by a famous reporter, stating, "I have received information from reliable sources that Prime Minister Léon Blum, Finance Minister Olivol, and Minister of National Economy Spinasse discussed monetary issues several days ago. Spinasse advocated lowering the value of the currency, while Olivol firmly opposed it, but said that this move would be considered separately if an understanding was reached with the gold bloc countries and the United States and Britain." The communist party's organ newspaper, L'Humanité, said, "Some parties have already begun to attack the franc, and some newspapers have also advocated devaluing the franc. Our party must demand that the government use extremely severe means to deal with these pranksters." (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Washington) Republican Senator Vandenberg, who has often criticized the New Deal, sent a letter to Treasury Secretary Morgenthau today, stating that the huge amount of foreign investment in the United States may cause adverse economic consequences. Vandenberg said that the total amount of foreign investment in the United States has reached 40,000,000,000 US dollars, which has made a large part of the financial organization and price organization of the United States dependent on foreign judgment. In 1931, foreign investors withdrew their investments, which made the US economy even more depressed. Vandenberg believed that buying cash at high prices was the reason for creating this kind of international investment situation and predicted that the European situation would disrupt the US economic situation. After receiving Vandenberg's letter, the Treasury Secretary immediately replied that once the political disturbances in Europe and the Far East are settled, a part of the funds will probably still flow out, at which time the United States will benefit directly and indirectly. Even if there is a large amount of cash exports in a certain period, it will not affect the credit foundation of the United States. The federal government's current cash reserves cannot be allowed to be collected by private individuals, and the economic situation this year is also very different from 1931. In the past two years, the United States had a cash surplus of 2,956,000,000 yuan, which exceeded the total gold production in the world, excluding the United States, by 181,000,000 yuan. (National Telegram, 24th)

Suspect in the Assassination Attempt on the US Chargé d'Affaires in Japan, Eiji Konno, Arrested Tonight

Sino-Japanese Investigators Land to Investigate the Nakano Case in Beihai; Guangdong Army's Tan and Wu Divisions Take Over Defense of Beihai; Eight Japanese Warships Gather Off the Port of Beihai Awaiting Orders

Guangzhou dispatch: After Li Zongren returned to Guangxi and ordered the withdrawal of Weng Zhaoyuan's troops stationed in Beihai, Weng's troops were ordered to first withdraw one regiment stationed in Lianjiang to Bobai on the Guangxi border starting on the 20th. The 159th Division of the 4th Route Army of Guangdong Province, led by Tan Sui, entered Lianjiang on the 21st to take over the defense. Mr. Xin, the former magistrate of Lianjiang County, entered the city with Tan's division to handle the aftermath. As for the Guangxi army stationed in Beihai and Hepu, they began to withdraw successively on the 21st. The Guangxi army here was the Independent 1st Division under Weng Zhaoyuan and the 61st Division under Qiu Zhaochen. On September 18th, the people of Beihai held a memorial meeting for the "September 18th Incident," and the atmosphere was tense. Fortunately, the garrison was on guard, so no more accidents occurred. When they were ordered to return to their garrison on the 20th, the Weng and Qiu divisions successively withdrew to the Guangxi border. On the same day, Tan's division also sent the Luo Cequn brigade to station in Anpu and Huangjinxu. The regiments of Pan Biao and Zhao Guanlan advanced along Gongguanxu and Qichangsi to Beihai and immediately issued a notice to reassure the people. As for the 154th Division under Wu Jianxiong, which continued to advance to the south, it also advanced to the Huaxian, Dianbai, Shuiche, and Maoming areas on the 23rd to coordinate defense with Tan's division. On the 21st, the entire Beihai area was completely taken over by the Guangdong army's Tan division. Ling Shifen, a special envoy sent by the Anfu warship to investigate the Nakano case, landed on the afternoon of the 22nd, requested the defending army to send a team to protect him, and contacted local gentry and merchants to discuss the progress of the investigation. On the morning of the 23rd, he telegraphed Jizhu Teiji, the Japanese vice-consul stationed in Guangdong, and Japanese staff member Songfu Hirohito, who were on the Sagano warship, to land together. Tan Sui, the commander of the division, and Xu Rangxuan, the chief of staff of the division, personally went to Beihai that day to order the maintenance of order. Ling Shifen, Yang Bingnian, Jizhu Teiji, Songfu Hirohito, and other Sino-Japanese investigators of the Nakano case were entertained by all sectors of the Beihai city gentry and merchants, and the details of the unfortunate incident that day were reported in detail. The Sino-Japanese investigators also inquired about the case in detail and summoned the suspects in the case one by one for questioning. It will take several days to investigate the case clearly before returning to the province to report. Sino-Japanese diplomatic agencies will begin negotiations based on the investigation report. It is said that the coffin of the deceased Nakano Shunzo was temporarily placed in a vegetable garden outside Beihai City after being coffined and buried. It is not yet known whether the coffin was opened for examination. After Nakano's death, his son Nakano Kiyoshi was still studying at Hepu Middle School, and his eldest daughter Tsuruko was still managing the Maruichi store. The Nakano family has completely become Chinese. Nakano Shunzo spoke the local dialect on weekdays, no different from a scholar, so he occupied a considerable position in Beihai society. His Maruichi store was located on Zhuhai Middle Road in the city. In 1926, it was once robbed by bandits. Nakano relied on foreign power and eventually obtained tens of thousands of yuan in compensation for the loss. After that, the store expanded even more, selling not only Western medicines but also foreign groceries, and serving as the Beihai manager of the Japanese Osaka Shosen Company. After Nakano's death, the Japanese side paid close attention to it. In addition to sending investigators on the Sagano warship first, it is said that eight Japanese warships have sailed to Beihai and gathered at the mouth of the Beihai Sea, including the Wakatake, Kuma, Yūbari, Ōtaka, Fuyo, Kaya, and Asagao. Except for the Sagano, which sailed from Guangzhou, the rest were directly sent by the Japanese Naval Province. It is said that the soldiers on the ships are preparing every day. (September 24th)

Hankou Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs the Executive Yuan and Ministry to Request Extension of the Implementation Period for Income Tax; Provincial Federation of Commerce Also Telegraphs Beijing for a Unified Demand

Hankou dispatch: The Hankou City Chamber of Commerce believes that the government has already decided to start collecting income tax on October 1st and January 1st of the 26th year of the Republic, respectively. However, October 1st is during the eighth month of the lunar calendar, right after the harvest season when businesses are busy operating. January 1st of next year is during the first month of the lunar calendar, far from the end of the year. If the tax is collected on schedule, businesses will be uneasy. In addition to sending letters to various industries the day before yesterday, requesting a unified demand to extend the implementation to March 1st of next year, it also telegraphed President Jiang of the Executive Yuan, as well as Ministers Kong and Wu of the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, yesterday, requesting them to consider the difficulties of businesses and approve the request. The Provincial Federation of Commerce will also make a unified demand. The telegram from the Hankou Chamber of Commerce is recorded as follows: To President Jiang of the Executive Yuan in Nanjing, Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, and Minister Wu Jun of the Ministry of Industry: We received the Hankou Municipal Government's forwarded implementation rules of the Provisional Income Tax Law, as well as an explicit order stating that income from the second category of salaries and remuneration for public officials and income from the third category of interest on public bonds and deposits will be collected starting from October 1st of the 25th year of the Republic, while all other items will be collected starting from January 1st of the 26th year of the Republic. We are to be informed, etc. Upon receipt of this, the association carefully studied the Provisional Income Tax Law and found that the tax rate was harsh and detailed, so we had to request modification. Business resources are exhausted, so we had to request a postponement of implementation. On August 21st, we listed the facts, reasons, and various difficulties, and submitted a request for approval. However, this case is of great importance to business operations. At a time when commerce is declining and people's livelihood is withered, we still earnestly ask you to observe the situation and approve our previous request. On the one hand, modify the tax rate and postpone implementation to alleviate business difficulties and relieve the people's plight. In the unlikely event that it is difficult to postpone in order to organize national revenue, then collecting in stages on October 1st of this year and January 1st of the 26th year of the Republic will cause great disturbances in the business community. This is because October 1st is during the eighth month of the lunar calendar, right after the harvest season when businesses are busy operating. January 1st of next year is during the eleventh month of the lunar calendar, far from the end of the year. If income tax is collected on schedule, businesses will be uneasy. The association speaks for businesses, and its pain is indescribable. We should request a unified extension to March 1st of the 26th year of the Republic, so that the business community can get used to it, and after the end of the year, all industries can proceed in an orderly manner without much worry. This is what the association is eagerly praying for. We respectfully submit this telegram, hoping that you will consider it. Hankou City Chamber of Commerce bows respectfully.

Japanese Embassy Sends Personnel to Hankou to Investigate the Yoshioka Incident; Written Record of Foreign Eyewitnesses; Japan Disregards It in Hankou

Hankou dispatch: Since the Yoshioka incident occurred, the Japanese authorities have begun investigating and our officials have assisted in arresting the murderer with great enthusiasm. However, the Japanese side, based on the confession of Liu Ya, a peddler arrested who is only eight years old, insists that the case occurred on a Chinese street and that the murderer was a man in his thirties wearing a blue short-sleeved shirt, believing that he was harmed by a Chinese. Therefore, they have increased troops in the Hankou River and tightened security. Consul General Miura and Vice-Consul Shirai, stationed in Hankou, also visited Governor Yang Yongtai of the provincial government on the 22nd and expressed their views. The truth of this case has become even more elusive. Our officials have made the greatest efforts to assist in the investigation. After investigation, a very important eyewitness has been found. The person's name has not yet been announced, but it is known that she is a female national of a northern European country. At the time of the incident, she was traveling by rickshaw from Hejie in the Japanese Concession to the Meifu Wharf. When she was about six or seven zhang away from Yoshioka's post, she suddenly heard two gunshots and saw Yoshioka fall beside his post. After the incident, the rickshaw continued to move forward and passed by the body. She saw an elderly stallholder and a child, startled by the gunshots, running down Hejie. She did not see anyone in a blue short-sleeved shirt. The circumstances she described were very clear and consistent with the testimony of Huang Qingyun, an elderly stallholder. This proves that Yoshioka's death was indeed beside his post, that the body was not moved after death, and that the murderer's entry and exit route must have been from Dazheng Street in the Japanese Concession, without any doubt. After hearing her statement, our officials wrote a record and officially requested the Japanese side to send personnel to the consulate of the country to which the person belonged to jointly inquire about everything. However, after receiving the letter, the Japanese side declined on the grounds of being too busy and did not send anyone. A second letter was sent, but there was no response. A third request was made for them to set a date themselves, but it was not approved. However, based on Liu Ya's confession, on the 22nd, Zhang Jinghuai, secretary of our municipal government, Wang Yufen, chief inspector of the Public Security Bureau, and Dong Kerene, section chief, went to the Japanese police station at the invitation of the Japanese police station to verify the record. The Japanese side did not agree with the foreign eyewitness's statement. On the same day, Liu Ya and Huang Qingyun were questioned for the second time. Huang's statement was the same as before, but Liu's statement had some discrepancies, which shows that the child is ignorant and his words are not credible. After the questioning, the Japanese side asked Zhang and others to sign, but Zhang and others refused because their task was only to verify the record, not to hold a joint trial, and there was no need to do so. Our side believes that the foreign person's statement is sufficient as a clue for the development of this case and is conducting an independent investigation in order to get to the bottom of it. Also, according to the report of the Japanese Embassy and the Japanese Consulate in Hankou, Mori Shima-shuto, a first-class secretary, was specially dispatched from Beijing on the 23rd to Hankou by China Aviation plane to investigate the truth of this case and to discuss the progress with Consul General Sanpei and Vice-Consul Shirai. It is still difficult to predict how the situation will develop in the future. (September 23rd)

Songjiang: Telegraphic Request to Abolish Housing Donation

The county's business and shop housing donation has been in effect for many years. Recently, according to provincial orders, a household housing donation will be organized, with the rent as the standard. If the household is self-produced, the valuation ratio will be used. First, the police will be sent to carry a survey form to investigate each household, to find out the number of rooms in the house, the value, and the amount of rent in great detail. However, those who do not understand the truth are generally panicked. The county's Chamber of Commerce, regarding this case, telegraphed the Ministry of Finance and the provincial government and civil administration of this province today, stating: The Songjiang local authorities recently sent police officers to arbitrarily assess the value of housing, saying that they wanted to expand police funding and add household housing donation. Merchants were shocked and residents were horrified, telling each other with frowning brows and uneasiness. At a time when the countryside is collapsing and all industries are declining, and relief is too late, how can we pile things on top of each other and add burdens? It is difficult to accept such illegal and harsh levies. We earnestly request that the housing donation be abolished by explicit order as soon as possible to alleviate the suffering.

Bawo Township Banditry Case Cracked

Wu Huiyuan and Guan Yuandi, wealthy brothers from Bawo Township, First District of this county, lived together in one house. They were robbed in July of this year. The owner was kicked in the abdomen by the robbers and the women's lower bodies were burned. The crimes were very heinous. The Public Security Bureau ordered a strict arrest, but the case was not solved for a long time. Yesterday, Yang Shijie, the detective captain of the Public Security Bureau, learned that the suspect Xu Daguizi was hiding in Tianmashan Town, so he went to the Seventh Resident Police Station to arrest Xu. Xu confessed that Xu Xiaohuzi was the leader and that the gun was also supplied by him. He is now hiding in the house of Zhou Ji in Wangjiafen Mountain, Rihuigang, Shanghai. Detective Yang led detectives Wei Yunhui and Zhang Yunxiang and set off at 4:00 AM this morning, arriving at Rihui

Private Soil Found in Car

Yesterday, the No. 9 car of the Shangsong Company, which returned from Shankai, was searched by soldiers of the Shanghai Security Team at Beiqiao. Private soil was found in the seat cabinet of the driver, Shen Jinfu, packed in a mooncake box, weighing eighty taels. It was taken back to the county government and transferred to the Third District Security Command for interrogation on suspicion of private trafficking. According to Shen Jinfu, who lives under the Maluqiao embankment in this city, he did not know it was soil and it was sent by a friend.

Nanhui: Robbery and Murder by Ruthless Bandits

Lu Jianting's house in Bian Sha, Sixth District, was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits on the evening of the 21st. Each held guns and knives and broke down the door. At that time, Lu's long-term worker, Chen Quanjing, was not yet asleep. He tried to rush out to call for help, but was shot and killed by a bandit. Lu was frightened by the sight and could only allow the bandits to rummage through the boxes, stealing one hundred pearls, sixty-five yuan in banknotes, several gold ornaments, and many clothes. Also, Zhang Dequan's house in Xiukang Township, Fifth District, was invaded by more than ten bandits the night before. Zhang's wife was injured in the head and other parts with wooden sticks. Twelve yuan in foreign currency and gold ornaments and clothes were stolen. Afterwards, Wang Julin, the township chief, and Sun Yunda, the patrol officer of the Zhoupu Public Security First Resident Police Station, jointly inspected and reported the case for investigation.

Kunshan: Continued Detention of "Xiang Hua" Relatives

More than ten young people in this county, including Gong Wei, Shi Chengzhe, Xu Zhenya, and Sheng Xichang, published the "Xiang Hua" bi-monthly, which contained slander. County Magistrate Peng issued a handwritten order to the Public Security Bureau to investigate and arrested Xu Zhenya, Sheng Xichang, and Gong Wei one after another. On the 24th, Lu Qianyuan, Zhou Zuzhen, and Ma Chiju, relatives of the journal, were also summoned. After interrogation, Lu Qianyuan was released on bail due to illness, and the remaining two were detained pending transfer.

Wujiang: Security Team Soldiers Cause Trouble Again

On the afternoon of the 23rd, at about 8:00 PM, dozens of soldiers from the 34th Company of the 9th Team of the Provincial Security Team stationed in this county surrounded and violently beat Yang Shushi, the Wujiang correspondent of the Suzhou Early News, inside the county government building. They punched, kicked, and knocked him to the ground. Although Yang Bin, the company commander of the team, tried his best to stop them, the people were too numerous and loud, and to no avail. Later, the county government received the news and sent Wu Juxin, the director of the Wujiang County Vagrant Training Center, to rescue Yang and send him to the County Hospital for treatment. The injuries were very serious. It is said that the reason was that the Early News published that Director Xu was promoted to the province as the security of the two companies, requesting the establishment of a training director, which led to the soldiers misunderstanding and causing a mass beating. Now the Early News has specially sent Yan Yisheng to Jiang on the 24th to express his condolences and plans to telegraph the province and county to severely punish the ringleaders.

Wuxi: Restriction on Slaughterhouse Fees

The Wuxi County Slaughterhouse, founded by Jin Decai, chairman of the local beef industry association, has been operating since the first day of July in the lunar calendar. Statistics show that it can slaughter about 20 heads per day. For outside beef cattle entrusted to the slaughterhouse for slaughter, a fee of 6.4 yuan per head is required (including 2 yuan in business tax), and the meat price is raised without authorization. Therefore, ordinary beef merchants are suffering from this heavy blow in this depressed society and are living a difficult life. Yesterday, the owners of various wholesale stores once gathered to discuss and decided to jointly ask the beef industry association to convene a members' meeting to discuss the meat price issue and ask for justice and appeal to the party and government agencies for relief in order to maintain business difficulties. At the same time, the provincial government instructed the county government to restrict the charging methods of the slaughterhouse, stipulating that the fee for each cattle should be one yuan and the fee for slaughtering a sheep should be two jiao, and no arbitrary overcharge should be allowed to show the restriction. After receiving the order, Magistrate Long immediately notified the slaughterhouse to comply.

Three Ruthless Bandits Captured

The Second Longzhu Temple in Zhoujing Alley was robbed by seven or eight bandits late at night on the tenth day of July in the lunar calendar this year. Pu Yi, the abbot, was held by the bandits and stabbed in the leg with scissors for shouting for help. After the incident, he reported to the Public Security Bureau for investigation and arrest. The day before yesterday, Wang Zhongyun, the captain of the detective team, received a secret report saying that the bandits who robbed the Longzhu Temple, Gao Abaobao, Deng Achun, and Zhang Xianggen, were hiding in Shijishang, Zhoujing Alley. After receiving the report, Captain Wang led detectives to the countryside to arrest them and arrested the above three criminals. One dan of wheat, five or six sheng of white rice, 20 yuan in legal tender, and dozens of pieces of clothing, all stolen goods, were found at Deng Achun's house and taken to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Changzhou: Suicide by Drowning and Then Slitting Throat

Sun Rugui, a 37-year-old man from Guizhou dressed in a black suit and sneakers, arrived at Yudaibian bridge in Wu County at around 4 p.m. on the 24th. He was looking nervous and unstable. He first took off his hat and threw it into the river, then threw himself into the river to drown himself. However, the river was very shallow and he did not drown. At this time, Sun Rugui took out a razor blade from his side and stabbed himself hard in the throat, causing blood to splatter everywhere. He fell into the water. Soon, a watchman passed by and was horrified by the sight. He immediately joined forces with nearby police officers to rescue him from the water. Because the bleeding from his throat did not stop, he was unconscious and was hired by car to the Wujin Hospital for treatment. The doctor inquired about his name and age, and he did not answer at first. When asked about the reason for his suicide, he was unable to speak and only wrote the words "harmed by a friend" with a pencil. He died of his injuries at about 6 p.m., which was also tragic.

Yangzhou: Demise of Elderly Gentleman Wang Jingtong

Mr. Wang Jingtong, who served as chairman of the Jiangdu County Chamber of Commerce and standing committee member of the Jiangsu Provincial Federation of Commerce, suddenly passed away at 2:00 PM on the 24th at his private residence on the Tudi embankment outside the South Gate due to a stroke. Wang originally opened an oil mill on the Tudi embankment outside the South Gate for many years. His family was originally well-off. Since Wang managed the business, his living standards have increased day by day, so that today, there is little family property left. When Chang Sun Chuanfang retreated to Jiangbei, the local area was chaotic and no one maintained the county administration. Therefore, Wang successively took over the official seal for three months. After the national army settled Jianghuai, Wang was once elected as a representative to the National Assembly and obtained membership in the Chinese Kuomintang. In this election, he also participated in the Jiangsu Provincial Vocational Group Chamber of Commerce election and had already obtained the preliminary election qualifications. However, during the prior efforts to solicit and contact people, he was often exposed to the wind and rain, so he may have overworked himself, which led to a stroke a few days ago. At that time, he was unconscious. After the best efforts of Chinese and Western doctors, he finally stabilized a little. He suddenly suffered another stroke on the morning of the 24th, and eventually died at 2:00 PM. It is said that Wang was 57 years old. His wife died three years ago. He currently has four concubines living inside and outside the city. His two sons have now started their own families. When the bad news came, everyone mourned the loss of a local talent.

Hangzhou: Joint Transport for Viewing Tide

As the Mid-Autumn Festival in the lunar calendar is approaching, the Zhejiang Highway First District Management Office notes that the Haining tide is particularly large. Last month, the stone railings, iron chairs, and part of the civilian houses in the coastal park were destroyed by huge waves. The Haining County Government specially raised funds from all parties to repair them in order to attract viewers. The Highway Bureau also applied to the Construction Department for an appropriation of 200 yuan and hired workers to rush to build a viewing platform with seats for 600 people. It also allocated 40 large buses to meet the needs. On the one hand, it has reached an agreement with the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway to handle joint transport. Joint tickets have been printed and delivered to the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway for sale. Joint transport special trains will run for four days starting on October 1st. When the first and second express and ordinary trains from Shanghai arrive at Chang'an Station, the Highway Bureau will send cars to pick them up and return on the same day.

Ningbo: More Than 10,000 Jin of Smuggled Salt Seized

Zhu Dehui, a private salt suppression supervisor of the Yuyao Salt Administration Inspection General Office, received a tip that private smugglers were secretly transporting a large amount of private salt for export at the mouth of Hangzhou Bay. He led a team of police to arrest them. However, the private smugglers opened fire and resisted arrest. After a long struggle, the private smugglers were defeated and sailed away. A total of more than 10,000 jin of private salt were seized from two large seagoing ships, and a private smuggler named Zhang Rengui was arrested and sent to the court for interrogation.

Yunyi Causes Trouble at Sea

Wang Shanben, Wang Shanzhong, and Wang Shanqing, rice merchants from Chen Zhao, Xiangdong, always transported rice to sea for profit every time the autumn harvest arrived. This year, he and He Hongcheng and others, rice merchants from Haidun, transported 60,000 jin of grain to sea. This was known to Lu Xinlan and other villagers, who reported to the militia team to stop them because the people's food was at stake. However, the Wangs took preemptive action, inviting many people in the industry and gangsters, intending to resist. The team members returned to the team when they saw that they were outnumbered. Yun Guantou, an old farmer watching, was severely beaten. Later, Captain Zhang led the team to arrive, and the crowd dispersed. Wang Shanzhong, the murderer, and Lu Xinlan, the reporter, were taken to the county for interrogation. Yun Guantou was reported to the county by his son to verify the injury.

Haizhou: Township Chief Kills Out of Spite

Du Pusheng, the township chief of Hufang Township, Third District of Guanyun County, and Qiao Jipei, the village chief, had a long-standing feud and had long wanted to frame Qiao. Therefore, they took advantage of the repair of the Liutanghe dike and induced Du Chenghuan, the village chief of the Sixth Ward, Du Chengfang, the village chief of the Seventh Ward, Ge Zhendong, the village chief of the Eighth Ward, and Ge Youqing, the village chief of the Ninth Ward, to stamp a blank official document, saying that the repair of the Liutanghe dike was urgent and that they should first stamp the blank official document so that it could be taken to a certain place for negotiation. The village chiefs did not suspect that it was a public matter and stamped it. Unexpectedly, the township chief took a blank official document back and immediately filled it in with the fact that Village Chief Qiao was harboring his brother-in-law, Zhuo Fei, in Wang Shankui, and reported it to the provincial security team stationed in Xin'an Town. The team then sent a team to arrest Village Chief Qiao and Wang Shankui. Township Chief Du shot and killed Wang in front of the village. Now Qiao's family has reported to the county government and requested an inspection to redress the injustice. It is said that the county government has sent personnel to inspect yesterday.

British Correspondence: Anglo-Egyptian Military Alliance Treaty Established

— Feng Lieshan

With just over 46 million people, including the Scots, the United Kingdom proper rules over more than 400 million colonial subjects, becoming a world power where the sun never sets. How could the British not feel they are the most superior race in the world! Forty years ago, the British politician Joseph Chamberlain said: "I believe that the British people are the greatest ruling race the world has ever known." You can still see this view on every Englishman's face today. However, they will never say it to your face. Perhaps this is where the British race excels! Even though they rule over you, you don't think they are so bad, at least not the worst.

Seeming weak and incompetent is the second special trait of the British. Throughout history, many have predicted the inevitable collapse of the British Empire. But to this day, the empire remains intact. And with each war, the British are the ones who profit the most. Before the European War, the Germans said:

"Can British soldiers even fight? Just let them run to Germany, and we'll send the police to catch them." The European War proved that even the German army didn't have the ability to catch them. The British never let their enemies underestimate them. Recently, Mussolini announced that Italy could mobilize eight million troops. Yet the British Empire's formal standing army is only about 200,000. If you focus solely on these numbers, you will be fooled again.

Many people criticize the British for being cold-blooded, unemotional, and selfish businessmen. Yet the British pride themselves on their ability to cope with their environment, yes, their ability to cope with their environment. Their actions may be a little slow, but just slow enough to be in time. During the European War, they promised independence to the colonial people, but after the war, they did not hesitate to use force to suppress the colonial people's independence movements. A few years ago, weren't the Egyptian Nationalists regarded as complete rebels in the eyes of the British? Today, in 1936, the British not only recognize the independence of Egypt under the rule of the Nationalists but also clink glasses with Egyptian diplomats and establish a military alliance treaty. You may think they have changed too much, but this is the characteristic of British politicians.

The Anglo-Egyptian treaty was facilitated partly by the efforts of the Egyptian Nationalists in their independence movement, but the most important reason was that Italy's occupation of Abyssinia forced the British to make this concession. When Italian troops invaded Abyssinia last year and fierce battles broke out, the British fleet mobilized and concentrated in the Mediterranean, sometimes attempting to encircle Italy. At that time, in terms of strength, Britain's leadership position in the Mediterranean was absolute. The Mediterranean fleet alone had more tonnage than the entire Italian navy. With the Suez Canal in British hands, British politicians advocated a tough stance against Italy, and seemed willing to resort to force if necessary. The League of Nations' economic sanctions against Italy were a product of this policy. However, all of this could not save Abyssinia from its fall. In the end, Mussolini triumphed, and the first to fail was none other than our British Empire!

This is the first and most tragic failure in the history of British diplomacy in centuries. We can see that British Foreign Secretary Eden first proposed lifting economic sanctions against Italy, which makes it clear how difficult Britain's situation is. Are the British really absolute pacifists? If the use of force could have maintained Britain's interests in Abyssinia, would the British have stood idly by and watched Italy swallow Abyssinia whole? Britain's failure this time was due to its overly conservative military preparations and its slow actions. The problem is that over the years, the British have not paid much attention to the new air force, while Italy has a large number of bombers. Theoretically, this batch of Italian bombers does not pose a great threat to the British Mediterranean fleet. Whether the air force can defeat the navy still lacks factual proof today. But the British finally softened. When the British Admiralty saw that their fleet was going to be the testing ground for this new type of warfare for the first time, they felt it was better to let Mussolini take a small advantage.

Italy's victory not only shook Britain's position in the Mediterranean but also threatened Britain's African colonies. Although Mussolini said that Italy was satisfied with obtaining Abyssinia and had no other extravagant desires, who dares to believe this statement! Britain's line of defense against Italy has shifted from the Abyssinia issue to the Egypt issue. This is something the British cannot sit idly by and watch if someone has ideas about the lifeline of their empire! The Suez Canal area. What the British are most worried about seems not to be Italy's eight million troops, but rather Italy secretly helping the Egyptian Nationalists' anti-British movement. Abandon Egypt, but be able to protect the Suez Canal, and they would rather abandon Egypt. This is the starting point of the Anglo-Egyptian treaty. After the treaty was signed, Egypt gained an independent country, and Britain gained a friendly army to help defend the Suez Canal. Now that the Egyptians have achieved their goal of independence, they not only have no reason to hate Britain, but on the contrary, protecting the Suez Canal and protecting their own country is their own business. The security of the Suez Canal has become the common destiny between the British Empire and Egypt. With this premise, the British were so generous in sacrificing many of the interests they had already gained. Therefore, British public opinion warmly welcomed the signing of the Anglo-Egyptian treaty. Only a few "die-hard" newspapers felt that Britain should not suffer such a loss. For example, the Morning Post said that Egypt cannot be talked about in terms of independence and autonomy. The only question is whether Egypt will belong to the Italians or the British in the future. Generally speaking, most British people recognize the value of this treaty. The Anglo-Egyptian Treaty was signed on August 26, 1936, at the British Foreign Office in London.

Local News

Municipal Government Proclamation on Harmonious Relations with Friendly Nations: Citizens are Urged to Strictly Comply

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai Municipal Government issued Proclamation No. 363, announcing the following: "In the way of governing the country today, we must first firmly adhere to discipline and strive for construction internally. Externally, we should respect national integrity and maintain harmonious relations with friendly nations. All our citizens must maintain friendly relations with friendly countries and must not have any words or actions that are xenophobic or incite ill will. This has already been clearly ordered by the Central Government and announced by this government. Fearing that some citizens may not fully understand this purpose, we hereby reissue this proclamation to urge all citizens to strictly comply. Those who dare to deliberately violate this will not be tolerated. This proclamation is hereby issued." September 24th, Republic of China, Mayor Wu Tiecheng.

Situation in Hongkou and Zhabei Eases: Meeting Held at Japanese Consulate Yesterday; Three Suspects Handed Over to the Court; Tian Gang's Body Cremated

According to the Central News Agency, after the incident on the evening of the 23rd of this month in which a Japanese sailor was attacked within the Public Concession, the Japanese Marine Corps stationed in Shanghai immediately dispatched troops to the intersection where the incident occurred and to the Zhabei area in the extra-settlement area to set up posts and inspect pedestrians. The situation at the time was very serious. Afterwards, the troops stationed at various intersections were withdrawn, and the extra-settlement posts were also withdrawn, except for a very small number still stationed at 63 Huayuan and Bazibqiao. The market has returned to its pre-incident state. Here is a follow-up report on the incident:

Withdrawal of Japanese Troops

The Japanese Marine Corps had set up posts in the Zhabei area of the city across the boundary after the incident. The municipal government filed a protest, and the Japanese Consul General, upon receiving our protest letter on the afternoon of the day before yesterday, withdrew a portion of the Japanese troops stationed across the boundary back to their units that evening. The withdrawal continued yesterday morning, and as of last night, all Japanese troops had been withdrawn except for a very small number stationed at 63 Huayuan and Bazibqiao on Jiangwan Road. The situation seems to have returned to its pre-incident state without any visible change.

Situation in Hongkou

A Central News Agency reporter patrolled the North Sichuan Road area yesterday and found that the situation was more relaxed than before. The Japanese troops stationed in the area where the incident occurred have also been withdrawn. However, a small number of Japanese troops are still stationed in front of the Taoyuan Dance Hall and near the Japanese barracks. Occasionally, Japanese armored vehicles patrol North Sichuan Road, but the level of alert is no longer very high. The site of the incident is still cordoned off with straw ropes, and pedestrians are prohibited from walking through. Only one or two Japanese remain on the sidelines to watch.

Zhabei is Quiet

A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency patrolled various parts of Zhabei yesterday, passing through Yokohama Bridge, Tongji Road, Jiangwan Road, Shuidian Road, Bazibqiao, and Tiantong'an, as well as the Hongkou area, without any obstruction. However, a small team of Japanese troops is still stationed in front of 63 Huayuan on Jiangwan Road, and one or two Japanese are patrolling back and forth. A small team is also stationed at the Japanese cemetery at Bazibqiao, with an armored vehicle parked in front of the gate. In addition, several Japanese soldiers guard the crossing of the Songhu Railway at Tiantong'an. The Japanese soldiers in various places no longer inspect pedestrians. On the concession side, in the Hongkou area, Japanese soldiers, either scattered or in formation, still patrol the streets. The Japanese troops at the Japanese elementary school near Arui Lane on North Sichuan Road and at the Taoyuan Dance Hall further south have not been completely withdrawn. The Japanese troops at the traffic control post at the Xiaocai Market on Wusong Road have been withdrawn, but there are still many Japanese troops stationed in front of the Japanese Club on the corner of Penglu Road. The residents of Zhabei are calm, and there have been no reports of any relocations.

Japanese Meeting

In addition to the two meetings held the day before yesterday, the Japanese consulate held another meeting of key military and naval personnel in Shanghai at the consulate office on Huangpu Road yesterday morning at 10:00, centered on Army Attaché Kita and Naval Attaché Sato. In addition to Kita and Sato, those present included Commander of the Third Fleet Okawa, Commander of the Marine Corps Kondo, and the full complement of personnel from the previous day's meeting: Counselor Wakasugi, First Secretary Tajiri, Intelligence Director Yoshioka, Consuls Fukui and Terasaki, Army Assistant Attachés Utsunomiya and Sagata, Special Service Agency Director Kusumoto, and Navy Assistant Attachés Okino and Minato. The meeting was devoted to discussing the aftermath of the incident and lasted for over two hours, not ending until 12:15. At around 4:00 in the afternoon, Wakasugi again convened a meeting of all consulate personnel, including Fukui, Terasaki, Secretary Nakata, Police Chief Kitamura, and Police Station Chief Tajima, which lasted for about an hour before adjourning.

Ma and Zhang Handed Over to the Court

The arrested suspects Ma Yongcai, Ma Yongnian, and Zhang Ronghe were sent back to the police station by the Japanese headquarters the night before last and handed over to the court for interrogation yesterday morning. However, the police station did not file a public prosecution but only requested that they be remanded in custody for further investigation. Therefore, the interrogation was rescheduled for October 3. Ma Yongcai, 30 years old, is from Jiading. His younger brother Yongnian, 27 years old, lives at No. 9 Ruiji Lane, Jiaxing Road. They both work at the Hongxing Printing Shop at No. 24 Ruiai Lane, 406 Lane, Shanhai Pass Road. Yongcai is a typesetter, and Yongnian works in printing. After 8:00 p.m. on the 23rd, the Ma brothers left the Hongxing Printing Shop after work to go home for dinner. When they arrived at the intersection of Haining Road and Wusong Road in front of the Willie Movie Theater, the incident of the Japanese sailor being attacked had already occurred, and traffic there was blocked. The two Mas could not proceed, so they changed their route to North Haining Road. Unexpectedly, they were also stopped midway. They then turned back and took a detour along a small alley. Unexpectedly, the entrance to this alley was the location of the incident. There were Japanese soldiers inside and outside the alley, maintaining strict vigilance. The two Mas were caught in a dilemma, hesitating in between, which drew the attention of the selected soldiers, and they were arrested by the Japanese soldiers and taken to the police station for questioning. Subsequently, the patrol officer stationed there reported the arrest of people along the way by the Japanese soldiers to the Hongkou Police Station. The police chief then ordered Chinese and foreign detectives to rush to the Japanese military headquarters to request that the two Mas be handed over to the police station for legal investigation. It was not until the morning of the 24th (the next day) at 10:30 a.m. that the Japanese authorities permitted the transfer of the Ma brothers to the detectives, who took them into custody at the Hongkou Police Station. Zhang Ronghe, 21 years old, is from Taizhou and lives at No. 8 Xinruikang Lane, Dithville Road. He sells porridge for a living. At the time of the incident, his porridge stall was parked at the entrance of Lane 240, South Haining Road, about five or six zhang away from the place where the gunshots were heard. According to Zhang, he heard a total of four or five gunshots, and two of Zhang's fellow villagers, Chang Tai and Da Lazi, had set up food stalls two or three zhang away from the place where the gunshots were heard. Fearing that the two might be in danger, Zhang went to check on them shortly after the gunshots were heard and saw that they were both safe. He then walked to the yellow sand bucket at a nearby lane entrance. At that moment, Japanese Marines arrived to search the area and found a Mauser pistol in the sand bucket. Zhang was immediately arrested. The Hongkou Police Station sent detectives to the Japanese military headquarters to request his transfer. At 2:50 a.m. on the 24th, a pistol with the number 26352 or 2653 (the last digit of the gun number is either 2 or 3, which is difficult to identify) was found in Yuqingfang, West Haining Road. It has now been sent to the Public Works Department's Firearms Inspection Office for inspection along with the Mauser pistol. Yesterday morning at 9:00 a.m., the police station sent Chinese and foreign detectives to escort the two Mas and Zhang to the First Special District Local Court. Judge Zhong Qing and Prosecutor Zhang Zongru took their seats in the Third Criminal Court for interrogation. The police station's representative lawyer was Zhang Shizhu. Lawyer Zhang briefly described the incident and requested that Ma and the others remain in custody for further investigation. Judge Zhong then questioned each of them one by one. All three claimed that they did not know the reason for their detention. The two Mas also described how they were treated well after being detained at the Japanese military headquarters, but Zhang's right eye was purple and slightly swollen. After the court hearing, the judge ordered that Ma and the others be held in custody and rescheduled the hearing for October 3.

Tian Gang Cremated

The body of the Japanese sailor Tian Gang was cremated on the Izumo warship at 3:00 p.m. yesterday. The cremation was conducted by the ship's captain and all the ship's officers and men. Yoshioka, the intelligence director of the Japanese Embassy in Shanghai, and the consuls in Shanghai, Fukui and Terasaki, all attended the funeral. After the cremation, the remains were placed in a container. The date for transporting them back to Japan has not yet been decided.

Shanghai Bankers' and Money Dealers' Associations Discuss Implementation of Income Tax; Gather Members' Opinions First Before Submitting to the Ministry for Adoption; Ministry of Finance Approves that Interest on Pension Savings is Still Taxable

The income tax on interest from bonds and savings deposits is approved to be levied starting from October 1. The Central Direct Tax Preparation Office has entrusted the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, as well as the Postal Remittances and Savings Bureau, to collect the tax on its behalf. It has also sent Deputy Director Liang Hejun to various provinces and cities to explain the matter to the banking and money industries. The Shanghai Bankers' and Money Dealers' Associations separately convened executive committee meetings yesterday to discuss implementation procedures and study the opinions raised by member firms, in order to compile them and submit them to the Ministry of Finance for adoption. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce received a Ministry of Finance clarification that interest on pension savings is still taxable. The details are as follows:

Bank Meeting

The Shanghai Banking Association held its 13th Executive Committee meeting at its office on Hong Kong Road at 4:00 p.m. yesterday. Committee members Li Fusun, Du Yuesheng, Wang Boyuan, Song Ziliang (representing Zhang Zhuyu), Pan Jiufen, Yang Jiemei, Wu Weir, Zu Jigang, Zhang Peishen, Wu Yunzhai, and Hu Xianshi were present, totaling eleven people. Secretary-General Lin Kanghou was also present. Wu Yunzhai chaired the meeting, and Gu Chengan recorded the minutes. The chairman first reported on the Central Direct Tax Preparation Office's approval for the implementation of the income tax on interest from securities and savings deposits starting from October 1, as well as the discussions between Deputy Director Liang Hejun and the committee members. The discussion on how to implement the plan then began. Committee member Li Fusun and Secretary-General Lin Kanghou successively presented their opinions and discussed the written opinions submitted by the Banking Association and member banks. It was generally believed that there were many practical difficulties in implementing the income tax. It was decided to first hand it over to the executive committee members for research and to convene a temporary executive committee meeting again within the next week, inviting representatives from various banks to attend. After the opinions are approved, they will be submitted to the Ministry of Finance in the hope that they will be adopted. The meeting adjourned at 6:10 p.m.

Money Dealers' Meeting

The Shanghai Money Dealers' Association held its 24th Executive Committee meeting of the 3rd session at its office on Ningbo Road at 2:00 p.m. yesterday. Committee members Shao Yanshan, Lu Shuchen, Xu Wenqing, Ye Xiuchun, Liu Wuqiao, Shen Jingliang, Zhang Mengzhou, Zai Jiemei, Zhang Wenbo, Yan Dayou, and Wu Zilin were present, totaling eleven people. Qin Xiqing, manager of the Money Industry Reserve, was also present. Shao Yanshan chaired the meeting, and Ge Huaiqing recorded the minutes. The chairman first reported that the government had approved the implementation of the income tax on interest from securities and savings deposits starting from October 1. At the autumn managers' meeting on September 19, the association proposed to organize an income tax research committee, deciding on nine members, with three recommended by the managers' meeting, three recommended from the executive committee members, and three recommended from the member representatives. The managers' meeting has now recommended Pei Yunqing, Wang Huailian, and Qian Yuansheng as committee members. The executive committee members were asked to recommend three members, and Liu Wuqiao, Lu Shuchen, and Yan Dayou were nominated on the spot. In addition, member Zhixiang et al. submitted opinions to be studied by the income tax research committee, which will be submitted to the Ministry of Finance in the hope that they will be adopted in the future. Finally, other cases were discussed, and the meeting adjourned at 3:30 p.m.

Ministry of Finance Approval

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce previously telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, stating that it should be stipulated in the detailed rules for the implementation of the income tax that lump-sum pensions, retirement funds, and alimony used for savings and interest-taking should be exempt from taxation. The Ministry replied, "The chamber's thorough study of the provisional regulations on income tax and the detailed rules for the implementation of the provisional regulations on income tax is commendable. However, it is found that the income tax regulations stipulate tax exemption for pensions, retirement funds, and alimony for the disabled, laborers, and those unable to support themselves, originally to show consideration for the toiling masses. If such pensions, retirement funds, and alimony are lump-sum payments that generate interest, they have become a form of capital and are therefore not exempt from taxation. This matter is a matter of the legal system, and the detailed rules for implementation have already been promulgated and are scheduled to take effect on October 1, and it is inappropriate to change them rashly. The request should not be considered. This approval."
