Tobacco Leaf Industry Association's Letter to the Tax Affairs Bureau: Request for Flexibility in Unified Purchase and Sale

Following the Ministry of Finance's proposal to implement unified control over the purchase and sale of tobacco leaves, the Tobacco Leaf Industry Association has been appealing to various parties for adjustments. Yesterday, they sent another letter to the Tax Affairs Bureau, requesting revisions to the proposed measures. The details are as follows:

First, Implement Unified Control Starting with Xuchang Tobacco

Our country's tobacco production is divided into two types. One is American tobacco, also known as "smoked tobacco" or "Yankee tobacco," which is artificially reprocessed and can be used for cigarettes. The producing areas are Xuchang in Henan, Qingzhou in Shandong, and Fuyang in Anhui. However, Qingzhou's entire crop is purchased by Japanese merchants. Xuchang produces 60 million dan annually, with a price of 60 yuan per dan and a tax of 10 yuan 004 fen 3 li. This raw material is supplied to domestic cigarette factories for manufacturing and is sufficient for self-sufficiency. The other type is called native tobacco, also known as "earth tobacco," which is sun-dried and can be used as pipe tobacco. The producing areas are widespread throughout the country, but it cannot be used for cigarettes. The Tax Affairs Bureau previously convened a meeting of tobacco leaf merchants, resulting in a decision to implement unified control first in the Xuchang area. The measures include: (1) Establishing a joint government-merchant purchasing and selling organization with a capital of 5 million to 10 million, named the "Tobacco Leaf Unified Control Joint Stock Company," with government and merchant shares split equally, or government 40% and merchants 60%, with the merchant shares split equally between Chinese and foreign merchants. If insufficient, the preparatory office will supplement it. (2) Seeking opinions on market organization and management, with merchants properly establishing and implementing regulations. (3) The preparatory office will discuss and determine the boundaries of administrative and business operations. (4) The Tobacco Leaf Unified Control implementation sequence will begin with a trial run in Xuchang, Henan.

Request to the Tax Affairs Bureau for Flexible Handling

Our city's Tobacco Leaf Industry Association sent a letter to the Tax Affairs Bureau yesterday regarding the unified control of tobacco leaves, stating, "With utmost respect, on the 28th of last month, your bureau, acting on orders to prepare for the unified control of tobacco leaves, invited representatives from our association to participate in discussions. After respectfully listening to your insightful views, our representatives immediately convened a meeting of all members, adhering to the imperial will and conducting discussions. It was unanimously agreed that the government's move to regulate the production and sales of tobacco leaves, improve tobacco leaf quality, eliminate privately manufactured raw materials, develop legitimate commerce, and enrich national tax revenues through the unified control of tobacco leaves reflects the government's grand plan to benefit the nation and its people. Our industry should provide the utmost assistance and work together to achieve this goal. However, the establishment of a joint government-merchant purchasing and selling organization is purely for profit-making purposes and exceeds the administrative scope of the government's guidance and supervision of tobacco leaves. It is undeniable that the tobacco leaf industry has weak capital and is unable to participate. Even if it could participate, it would be inadvisable. Once this business organization with substantial capital is established, each tobacco leaf merchant with fragile economic strength will inevitably be eliminated. Even if a few can temporarily struggle to survive, they will have no business to conduct because tobacco leaf consumers will directly purchase from the large company. As a result, our long-standing tobacco leaf companies will be overthrown and unemployed due to the establishment of the joint government-merchant organization. The livelihoods of hundreds of thousands of people directly employed will be on the verge of extinction. Although the government has no intention of competing for profit with the people, tobacco merchants face the risk of total annihilation. Is this the government's original intention to protect merchants and benefit the people? In our humble opinion, if the government wants to achieve the goals of eliminating private manufacturing, enriching national taxes, regulating production and sales, and improving tobacco leaf quality, there are other ways besides the joint government-merchant purchasing and selling organization. If the government leads from above and merchants assist from below, working together, success is assured. We implore your bureau to consider the livelihoods of hundreds of thousands of people directly and indirectly employed in our industry and to abandon the idea of a joint government-merchant purchasing and selling organization. Under the principle that the government neither competes for profit with the people nor reduces tax revenue, while also not harming the interests of tobacco merchants, we can discuss measures and cooperate together. This is our sincere hope. We hereby submit this to the city and hope it will be accepted. We also request a reply."

Female National Products Visiting Staff Begin Work Yesterday, Explaining the Purpose to Families

The female visiting staff of the Shanghai National Products Promotion Association, including Xu Chengqing, Xu Songzi, Chen Yingfen, Lin Wen, and Shen Wenxian, began their visiting work yesterday. Under the major premise of protecting the country, people from all walks of life have mostly changed their views on foreign goods and are happy to use national products. This is truly a valuable phenomenon for the country. We often think that women are in charge of household affairs, and most of the household items are selected and purchased by women. Our female compatriots' patriotism will certainly not lag behind others. However, due to the inability to distinguish the authenticity of national products or unfamiliarity with the progress of national products, there are many cases of mistakenly purchasing foreign goods. Therefore, it was decided by public opinion to select and hire female visiting staff to go to families to talk, study with housewives to distinguish national products, and inquire about the housewives' criticisms of various national products, so that they can be passed on to the manufacturers for improvement. Our female compatriots understand the righteousness and will definitely agree with this initiative. We hereby state the purpose and request your consideration."

Chinese Economic Society Annual Meeting Opens Tomorrow, Members From All Over Report In, More Than Ten Papers Received

The 13th Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society is scheduled to open tomorrow at 9:00 AM at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA. Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Finance, and Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of this city, have all agreed to speak at the meeting. The attending representatives have already reported in yesterday, with an estimated 200 people attending. More than ten papers have been received from Ma Yinchu, Chen Xing, Li Quanshi, Zhang Sumin, Dong Xiujia, Chen Changxun, and others. All of them discuss fiscal and economic issues during extraordinary times. The central issue of the debate has been set as "Should China's new financial policy focus on stabilizing domestic prices or stabilizing foreign prices?" Notice

In ancient times, people used literature to make friends. In modern times, academic groups gather for meetings, and the intention is similar. Since its establishment, the Society has held annual meetings in various places for more than ten years, all of which have been welcomed by local people and valued by all sectors of the country. The Board of Directors decided to follow the resolution of the previous annual meeting and chose Shanghai as the location for the 13th Annual Meeting of Members. Its significance is undoubtedly important. In today's difficult times, the economic crisis is no less than the political one. Since the Society is committed to studying economics, it is our unshirkable responsibility to save the country from decline. Therefore, in the center of domestic finance and industry, we gather the members of the society to conduct a collective brainstorming session. The scope of the papers will be economic and financial issues during extraordinary times, and the topic of the debate will be new financial policies. It is believed that there will be insightful opinions that can inspire and awaken people. Whether in terms of the country and society or in terms of academic thought, there will be many benefits. Moreover, Shanghai is ranked fifth in the world, with convenient transportation by water and land. Talented people from all over the world gather here. The industry and finance lead the country, and the cultural construction can serve as a model. It is appropriate to visit and learn from it. If you find the Bund of Shanghai to be too secular, then the famous mountains of Wu are nearby. You can broaden your horizons and enjoy the scenery. A grand meeting is not always held, and a good opportunity should not be missed. All my comrades, why not come? I am sending you a brief note to invite you to the meeting.

Staff

Pacific Association: Celebration of the Discovery of the Pacific; President Kung Hsiang-hsi Attends and Delivers Speech; Hopes for Increased Friendship Among Pacific Rim Countries; Kuo Ping-wen Lectures on China's International Relations

The Pacific Association held a meeting at the Cathay Hotel yesterday at noon to commemorate the 423rd anniversary of the Spanish explorer Balboa's discovery of the Pacific Ocean and to foster friendly relations. Speeches were given by Kung Hsiang-hsi, Kuo Ping-wen, and others, making it a grand occasion. The details are as follows:

Guests Attending

Among those attending yesterday were over two hundred people, including envoys and consuls stationed in Shanghai, Chinese and foreign guests, and members. Chairman Hilmy Effendi delivered the opening remarks and reported on the congratulatory telegram from the Honolulu Pacific Association.

Kung's Speech

Subsequently, Association President Kung Hsiang-hsi delivered a speech, translated into English by Chen Bingzhang. He stated, in essence: "On behalf of China, I am very honored to welcome everyone to this celebration of the discovery of the Pacific Ocean. Chairman Hilmy Effendi mentioned that the Chinese had already discovered the Pacific before the Spanish explorer Balboa. At that time, transportation was blocked, and international relations were very distant. Today, when we commemorate Balboa, we should not only commemorate his discovery of the Pacific but also hope for friendly and peaceful relations among the countries along the Pacific Rim. When Balboa discovered the Pacific, he did not anticipate today's development and changes. Today, the countries along the Pacific have become close neighbors. Due to political and economic ties, since the European war, the area has become one of the most important regions on Earth, known as the Pacific Century. Therefore, when we commemorate Balboa, we especially hope that the countries along the Pacific Rim will not engage in competition and division but will strive for cooperation and peace, which aligns with the Pacific Association's mission." Subsequently, the Swiss Consul-General, representing the consular corps in the city, delivered a congratulatory speech.

Kuo's Lecture

Following this, Shanghai Association President Kuo Ping-wen delivered a lecture on "China's Current International Relations," stating, in essence: "In the past, due to geographical, cultural, and other factors, China overestimated itself, and transportation between East and West was not yet convenient, leading to isolation and difficulties in the early development of Sino-foreign relations. However, today, land, sea, and air transportation have developed rapidly, and the past barriers have disappeared. China's disputes, economic, and cultural relations with friendly nations have become closer. Furthermore, China is actively pursuing reform, and unequal treaties that hindered China's sovereignty in the past are now being revised. In recent years, concessions and leased territories have been returned, and treaties based on equality and mutual benefit have been repeatedly signed. At the same time, the Chinese government is also working to adjust diplomatic relations based on the principles of equality and mutual benefit. In terms of culture, since the opening of maritime transport, China's absorption of other cultures has kept pace with the times. In recent years, Western countries have also made significant progress in the study of Chinese culture, such as poetry, songs, drama, art, and so on. Economically, in recent years, due to the development of various transportation and industrial enterprises, China has become one of the world's most important markets for machinery and industrial raw materials. This point has attracted the close attention of various countries. At the same time, with the recent boom in domestic construction, industrial development, agricultural improvement, and quality enhancement, China's exports will also make significant progress, it can be asserted. Now, let me analyze the individual relationships between China and important countries. China and Britain have always maintained friendly relations. The newly appointed Ambassador Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen has a far-sighted view. I believe that he will make greater contributions to promoting Sino-British relations. The relationship between China and the United States has been harmonious for more than 150 years. During my recent visit to the United States to study international trade, the impressions I gained were also very good. As for China and Japan, due to their shared culture and ethnicity, there is indeed a need for coexistence and co-prosperity. However, the realization of friendly relations between the two countries depends on mutual deep understanding and frank and sincere consultation. Economic cooperation is also welcome, but it must be based on the principle of mutual respect for sovereignty. I recently saw an article by Mr. Sogawa Shinji in a Tokyo dispatch, which stated: 'If we hope that China and Japan will join hands to consolidate peace in East Asia and enhance the well-being of the two peoples, and Japan hopes that China will change its attitude towards Japan, then the direction of Japan's national policy should also be changed.' This is truly an insightful view. It can be seen that the Japanese intellectual community is deeply aware that improving its policy towards China is the most important task at present. The improvement of relations between the two countries in the future will also depend on this. As for China's attitude towards the goals of the League of Nations, it has always expressed sympathy. For more than ten years, it has enthusiastically participated in various undertakings of the League of Nations. Although some people have recently been disappointed with the League of Nations, the League of Nations is not a supreme government but only a permanent organization in international life that contains significant moral force. Therefore, the Chinese government continues to cooperate closely with the League of Nations. Recently, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has repeatedly sent specialists to serve in the League of Nations office to promote various economic, political, and technical cooperation between China and the League of Nations. Due to time constraints today, I am unable to discuss various international relations and the work of various organizations in detail, but I firmly believe that the enhancement of friendship between countries must be based on mutual understanding. The purpose of this association now is to promote friendly relations between China and other Pan-Pacific countries. Today, we are holding a commemorative banquet for the discovery of the Pacific, and we should have a clearer understanding. I have expressed my thoughts and feelings and humbly request your guidance and encourage each other. I hope that everyone will contribute to the best of their ability, how fortunate that would be."

Zhabei Maternal Heart Hospital Opens Today; Founded by Lu Bohong and Others; Special Free Clinic Established

The Zhabei area is vast with many residents, mostly from the laboring class. Although there are several hospitals in the area, they are still insufficient. In view of this, Lu Bohong, a prominent figure in Shanghai's business and charity circles, acquired more than 20 mu of land in the Niuqiaowan area of North Baoxing Road in Zhabei to build the Maternal Heart Hospital. The necessary funds were provided by Lu from his 60th birthday gifts from friends and relatives. The shortfall was supplemented by Lu personally and by donations from enthusiastic philanthropists. The preparation has taken two years, and the entire project has now been completed. The design of the building and the internal layout are extremely complete. The chief physician is Dr. Song Wusheng, a well-known figure in the medical field. The resident physicians are Zeng Xianming and others. The opening ceremony is scheduled to be held at 3:00 PM today. An invitation to visit was issued in advance and Mayor Wu will be invited to inaugurate it. It is heard that the hospital has now begun accepting patients and has established a special number of free treatment slots to benefit the poor and sick.

Robbers Escape, Harming the Legal Police; Jiang Wanyuan Case Concluded; Key Forgotten in the Back Door Lock Hole; Debate Concluded, Awaiting Sentencing

On the morning of the 15th of this month, Special Court No. 2 escorted two robber prisoners, Wu Asan and Wang Agen, from the legal police to the waiting room behind the First Tribunal. At about 2:00 p.m. that afternoon, the two prisoners, Wu and Wang, took advantage of the legal police's negligence and opened the back door, broke the iron bars on the iron bucket, and escaped. Because Jiang Wanyuan, the 515th legal police officer in charge of the key to the waiting room, was negligent in his duties and forgot the key in the lock eye of the back door of the waiting room, causing the two prisoners to take the opportunity to open the door and escape. The 515th legal police officer Jiang Wanyuan was transferred to the Prosecutor's Office. After Prosecutor Wang Ren's investigation was concluded, he filed a public prosecution with the Criminal Tribunal of the same level for the crime of negligent escape under Article 162, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law and detained Jiang in the detention center awaiting investigation. These details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Chen Shuoying, together with Inspector Wang Ren, came to Criminal Court No. 2 for trial. First, the prosecutor stated the intention of the prosecution. Upon questioning, Jiang Wanyuan stated that at about 8:00 a.m. that morning, he escorted the prisoners to the waiting room. The court session began at 10:00 a.m. and adjourned at 1:00 p.m. He went back to lunch and handed the key to the 141st legal police officer. When he returned to the court, he first went to the writing room to register the prisoner. When he returned to the First Tribunal, he found that the prisoners had escaped. He did not forget the key in the lock hole of the back door. Although the key was in his charge, it was always hung on the window in front of the waiting room, and all the legal police could take it off and open the door to escort the prisoners, etc. The court also summoned the 141st legal police officer for questioning, ordered the debate to begin, and then announced the conclusion, awaiting the actual judgment. Jiang was still remanded in custody.

Respectfully submitted to the Fourth District Party Department of the Kuomintang Shanghai Special Municipality."

Public Concession Vehicle Committee Member Zhu Maocheng Answers Questions; Discusses Reducing the Number of Vehicles

The problem of rickshaws in the Public Concession has become tense again since the Public Concession Bureau decided to reduce the number of public rickshaws by 484 starting in March next year. Rickshaw owners have strongly opposed it, and opinions from all walks of life are also quite divided. However, the Public Concession Bureau authorities do not seem to have made a clear statement on the purpose and method of this decision to reduce the number of vehicles. The following is an excerpt of a conversation between Zhu Maocheng, a member of the Public Concession Rickshaw Affairs Committee, and a guest about the reduction of vehicles.

Purpose and Method of Reducing Vehicles

(Guest asks, same below) What is the purpose of the Public Concession Bureau reducing the number of vehicles, and what is the method? (Answer) Regardless of the traffic aspect, the current number of public rickshaws in the concession is actually too many in terms of the livelihoods of the rickshaw pullers. In fact, the current income of rickshaw pullers per shift, after paying the rickshaw rent, is very low. This is generally recognized by all walks of life, but the method of increasing their income is not very clear. It must be known that the total daily income of all rickshaw businesses in the concession is a certain amount of money. The more vehicles there are, the less income each rickshaw puller has. The logic is very clear. Therefore, one reasonable way to increase the income of each rickshaw puller is to reduce the number of existing rickshaws. At the same time, in consideration of the impact on rickshaw owners, the Public Concession Bureau has decided to reduce only 484 out of 9,984 vehicles starting on March 1 next year, to show sympathy. Although rickshaw owners will suffer a slight loss, the income of rickshaw pullers, if there are no unexpected developments, will increase by 5%.

Registering Rickshaw Pullers Will Not Cause Unemployment

(Question) Outsiders say that this decision to reduce vehicles will cause more than a thousand people to lose their jobs. What is your opinion? (Answer) This kind of speculation is not accurate, because according to the situation in recent years, only registered rickshaw pullers can pull rickshaws. Therefore, whether the number of vehicles is reduced or not, it has no relationship with unregistered rickshaw pullers. As for registered rickshaw pullers, according to the current plan of the Public Concession Bureau, there is no need to worry about unemployment. This is because the number of vehicles that the Public Concession Bureau has decided to reduce will be carried out within the scope of the natural reduction of registered rickshaw pullers. The so-called natural reduction refers to the number of people reduced due to death, old age, weakness, and change of profession. Among them, those who have been proven by the Public Concession Bureau are allowed to be supplemented. However, there are also a large number of people who are not known clearly. The exact number will be determined after the public rickshaw pullers in February next year have renewed their licenses. Therefore, under this situation, rickshaw pullers really have no worries about unemployment.

There Is No Intention to Destroy Rickshaw Owners

(Question) Outsiders say that reducing rickshaws has the suspicion of destroying the rickshaw business run by Chinese people and supporting the development of foreign tram and bus companies. What is your opinion? (Answer) This kind of rumor is really absurd, and sensible people will not believe it. In fact, rickshaws and trams and buses have long been impossible to compete with. Wherever there are trams and buses, rickshaws have long been unpopular with the public, especially in terms of distance. For example, when we go from Jing'an Temple to the Bund, in terms of car price and time, we always like to take a bus, and rarely hire a rickshaw. Whether the number of public rickshaws in the concession is 9,984 or 9,500, there is no impact on this point. In short, under the current phenomenon of supply exceeding demand for vehicles, rickshaw pullers will inevitably compete with each other for customers. As a result, everyone will not be able to eat their fill. Therefore, for the sake of the livelihoods of rickshaw pullers, the best way is to slightly reduce the number of vehicles within the limit of the natural reduction of rickshaw pullers, so that it is close to the number needed by the public, and rickshaw pullers can also enjoy the minimum standard of living.

The Work of the Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Society

Finally, when asked about the work of the Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Society, the answer was that recently, newspapers have often published criticisms from other circles about the Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Society, saying that it is of no benefit to rickshaw pullers, so the true value of the society is unknown to the outside world, which is a pity. On this point, I don't need to defend it. It is best for those who are interested in all circles to go to visit in person. Although there are places where the Mutual Aid Society needs to be improved, a fair observer, in view of the large scope of the Society's work, will inevitably regard it as the only labor welfare organization in the Far East. For example, from the 7th to the 13th of this month, within a week, rickshaw pullers attended the Society to participate in the meeting 64,837 times, including 3,914 people who went to the clinic to see a doctor, 24 people who asked a doctor to come out to see a doctor, 156 people who were served by itinerant nurses, 155 people who were treated in the Society's hospital, 356 people who were sent to other hospitals for treatment, 163 people who received reproductive guidance, 3,154 people who read books and listened to lectures, 15,555 people who listened to lectures and read books, 279 times of giving rice and funeral expenses to members and their families, 6 members' families who received death insurance, 13,602 people who bathed, 20,047 people who drank tea, and 22 cases of requesting mediation of disputes. These works are all approved by the real rickshaw pullers. At the beginning of May this year, there were as many as 30,000 rickshaw pullers who individually voted in favor of the work of the Society and expressed their willingness to pay membership fees in a few days.

Western Paint Industry Lawsuit: Settle Accounts After Disaster Relief; Directors Do Not Manage Accounts, When to Investigate; Ignoring a Difference of Hundreds of Thousands

The Shanghai Western Paint Industry Association sent representative Ma Shangjie and appointed a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the Second Special Court, accusing Le Zhenbao, Bei Runsheng, Zhang Lanping, and Le Gengrong of mismanaging the property of the Foreign Goods Commercial Association. The court has repeatedly held hearings to summon the parties, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00, Judge Chen Shuoying presided over the continued hearing in the criminal court. Both parties, accompanied by lawyers, appeared in court. The court first asked Ma Shangjie, "Which lawyers represent which defendants?" The plaintiff Ma said, "I represent Qin Dongliang and Chen Gengsheng." Lawyers Cao Kun and Hua Danhua said, "I represent Wang Zuolin, Hu Tongsheng, and Xia Gengsheng." Lawyer He Xiaoyuan said, "I represent Ding Fang'e, Dong Yuzhen, and Su Xiangxuan." Then Le Zhenbao was questioned. The court ordered them to submit the title deed and account books. Zhang Lanping first submitted a title deed (French Concession deed) to the court. Then, the defendant's defense lawyer, Li Zuyu, submitted two account books for the years 1933, 1934, and 1935. He also said that the defendants were directors and did not manage the accounts. The account books for the three years were submitted by the association's accountant, surnamed Feng. The court asked the plaintiff's side, "You requested to investigate the accounts from the establishment of the association until now. Why are only three years of account books submitted?" Li said, "The court did not specify which year's account books to investigate. However, the plaintiff must point out the specific facts of the defendant's embezzlement. After proof, the defendant can submit them. The accusations made by the plaintiff are empty and groundless. On what basis can the accounts be investigated?" The court said, "That is because the court ordered the submission of the accounts for the convenience of investigating the evidence." The court also asked Ma Shangjie, "Your accusation that the defendants have embezzled funds from the establishment of the association until now is too vague. You must present the facts of which year and which item." Ma replied, "In 1932, according to the standing chairman of the Western Paint Association, Chuan Jiemei of Gonghe Lai Paint Company, and Li Shuyan, the property in the association differed by more than 100,000. Later, we requested to investigate the accounts and receive income and expenditure reports, but they were ignored. Now, the defendants have submitted the account books, but they are missing two items: current account and miscellaneous items, and rent collection account. We will now investigate the accounts from 1912 to the present." Le Zhenbao and Zhang Lanping said together, "The association is not a store and does not have a current account or miscellaneous items. The current account is in the rolling account, and the miscellaneous items are in the total account. There is a separate account book for rent collection. If the court wants to see it, it can be submitted." At this point, the court ordered that the accounts submitted today were incomplete and there was nothing to question. The account books from 1912 onwards should be submitted to the court for further interrogation at a later date.

Another Case of Investigators Using Torture in the French Concession; Gong Renfa Falsely Accuses a Good Person of Theft; Wu Xiaogouzi Beaten and Injured

Wu Jiangfu, 53 years old, from Danyang, lives at No. 101 Xilin Road, Nanshi, and makes a living as a peddler. Wu's son, Wu Xiaogouzi, is 14 years old. Wu sent him to Yang Binglan (35 years old, from Zhenjiang), a tanner at No. 49 Olliehe Road in the French Concession, as an apprentice. Yang lives in the house and is a second landlord. On the 13th of this month, Xi Renfa rented Yang's pavilion room, agreeing to a monthly rent of five yuan. Xi moved in for nine days without paying the rent. Suddenly, on the afternoon of the 22nd, at about 4:00 PM, he claimed that Wu Xiaogouzi, Yang Binglan's apprentice, had stolen five yuan in banknotes and reported it to the French Police Station. A police officer surnamed Wang was dispatched to investigate and took Yang Binglan and Wu Xiaogouzi, master and apprentice, to the police station for questioning. They were released at about 9:00 PM that night. Yang and Wu, master and apprentice, were injured in the police station and went to Renji Hospital for treatment. Yang's injury was minor and he was discharged. Wu Xiaogouzi's injury was serious, with chills and fever, swelling all over his body, and mental disorder. His life may be in danger. The next day, Wu Jiangfu reported to patrolman No. 466, who reported it to the police station. The police station sent personnel to investigate, first sending Wu Xiaogouzi to the hospital for treatment, and then detaining Gong Renfa, who instigated the false accusation. Yesterday afternoon, he was sent to the First Criminal Division of the Second Special Court for questioning. The police department's lawyer requested a postponement of the investigation. The judge briefly questioned the defendant, Xi Renfa, and ordered a postponement for further investigation. Yang Binglan and Wu Jiangfu hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the court, requesting an examination of the injuries and accusing Xi and the investigators of falsely accusing a good person of theft, abusing their power, using illegal torture, and beating them into injury, requesting that they be punished according to law. The court will hold a hearing to summon the parties in the near future.

Shenxin No. 2 Factory Will Resume Production First; Chinese and Shanghai Banks Invest; Obstacles to the Resumption of Production at No. 5 Factory

The Shenxin Textile Company's No. 2 and No. 5 textile factories on Yichang Road and Huade Road in this city have been closed for a year and a half since the lunar New Year last year. The two factories originally operated with mortgages from Chinese and Shanghai banks, so the company and the banks suffered losses after the closure. This year, the cotton outlook is optimistic, so the two sides are negotiating to resume production. A Central News Agency reporter learned that the No. 2 factory is invested by the Chinese and Shanghai banks, with Chinese accounting for 60% and Shanghai accounting for 40%. The company's proposal to the two banks to resume production has been approved. However, the factory's machinery and equipment are relatively old, and the factory buildings are also not neat. Therefore, it is hoped that it can start work at the same time as the No. 5 factory, which has newer equipment. However, the factory still has debts to the Yongfeng Money Shop. The bank has now stopped lending and is unwilling to continue investing, and requires that the money it has lent be repaid first, which the two banks are unwilling to do. If it wants to transfer the debt, there is no suitable buyer for a while. Therefore, the proposal to resume production at the same time has been obstructed. Yesterday, the company sent a letter to the two banks asking them to resume production at the No. 2 factory first. The two banks are currently studying it and said that they can accept it and will negotiate soon.

After the implementation of the government's new monetary policy, it was ordered to transfer the issuance reserves to the Issuance Reserve Management Committee for acceptance. It was not until last month that the Hangzhou Branch of the Bank of China took over and transferred it to the Issuance Reserve Management Committee.

The bank believed that the Ministry of Finance stipulated that subsidiary coin notes should be issued by local banks in various provinces, so it submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance through the Finance Department, requesting approval to issue new subsidiary coin notes of 8 million yuan. Finance Minister Cheng Yuanfan also visited Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi to request results. Stipulated Reserves

A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency learned from the Shanghai Branch of the Zhejiang Local Bank yesterday that the new subsidiary coin notes are divided into three types: 10 cents, 20 cents, and 50 cents. After the approval order from the Ministry of Finance is issued, a printing company will be entrusted to print them. The reserve fund for the issuance of subsidiary coin notes is 60% cash (i.e., legal tender from the Central Bank of China, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications) and 40% mortgage (i.e., government bonds, etc.)

Dashing Amusement Park Opens Ao Mountain Lantern Display

As the Mid-Autumn Festival approaches, various amusement parks at sea are adding novel programs to decorate the festive season. For instance, the Dashing Amusement Park on Tibet Road sent specialists to Fujian a month ago to procure Ao Mountain Lanterns to please visitors. All the lantern figures, pavilions, towers, and flora and fauna are made of the most delicate five-colored silk, ingeniously lifelike and incredibly flexible. With mechanisms inside, they can rotate naturally, appearing vividly real. It is said that the lanterns opened by the park display the entirety of the Grand View Garden. All twelve of the Jinling Twelve Beauties and other important figures like Grandmother Jia and Granny Liu from "Dream of the Red Chamber" are present. Furthermore, around the Grand View Garden, nearly suburban landscapes, mountains, rivers, forests, and fields have been created, looking realistic. Moreover, an ancient emperor's hunting scene is depicted, with guards arrayed, horses circling, and bows drawn, vividly lifelike. Records show that Ao Mountain Lanterns were items of tribute for the inner court during the Qing Dynasty. Because of the money and manpower required for their production, they were beyond the means of ordinary wealthy families, so opportunities to see them were rare. The park has signed a contract with the Fujian Sanshan Jincheng Lantern Architecture Company, investing 7,000 yuan, and starting from the fourteenth day of this lunar month, all the newly made, precious lanterns will be displayed on the eighth floor of the park.

New Drugs for Treatment: Atebrin and Plasmoguine

Malaria eradication work is extremely difficult to achieve, as sewage is everywhere and the public's knowledge is largely limited. Therefore, fundamentally eradicating malaria mosquitoes and larvae is no easy task. Although the Bureau of Health is working hard on the issue of malaria eradication, it is difficult to simultaneously address the treatment aspect due to various reasons. Eradicating malaria cannot rely solely on mosquito control, as the number of mosquitoes cannot be completely eliminated by human efforts alone. It must be understood that all chronic malaria patients, if not cured, are a source of renewed malaria spread. Therefore, if a person with malaria is not cured, mosquitoes will have the opportunity to transmit the disease from that person to others. There is a clear example of this. When the Panama Canal was being dug, malaria was rampant. Initial attempts at various mosquito control methods were ineffective. Later, when all malaria patients were moved out of the infected area, the trend gradually declined. This is because the mosquitoes lost their source of malaria and could no longer spread the disease. In the past, quinine was considered a magic cure for treating malaria, but it could only treat the symptoms and not eradicate the malaria parasites in the body. Recently, there has been a misconception that malaria parasites hidden in the body can increase immunity, which is a misunderstanding of medical principles. If malaria is not cured, it is detrimental to the patient's health. Recently, British and German experts have invented two new drugs: Atebrin and Plasmoguine. These drugs have no side effects. Atebrin is particularly pure. Compared to quinine, the former has no side effects, and the course of treatment is very short, only five days. Plasmoguine has been used to treat malaria in the past, but it required large doses to be effective. Today, the properties of this drug are fully understood, and it can be used to kill Gametin (sexually reproductive larvae) with a very small dose (greatly reduced from before), which has a great effect, so there are no harmful effects. In severe cases, injection is even more effective.

Letters to the Editor

To the Editor:

I am writing to you regarding the news item "Haily Steamer Carries Strange Cargo" in today's local news section of your newspaper. The report is entirely false. Mr. Liu Kechun, manager of the Shantou business, traveled to Shanghai on the Haily steamer on the 20th. Xieji Sugar Factory in Shanghai entrusted him with four baskets of mud used to make local sugar. When landing, he forgot to take them with him. The captain of the Haily steamer did not investigate and jumped to conclusions, mistaking them for ammunition. It is truly absurd. In addition to proving the misunderstanding to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and retrieving the four baskets of sugar, I am writing to request that your newspaper investigate and correct the report and publish this letter to clarify the truth. Sincerely, Tong An Company, for the editors of Shen Bao.

To the Editor:

I am writing to you because your newspaper published on September 24 my resume as a member of the Brain Workers Advancement Association, for which I am extremely grateful. However, there is an error in the resume. The title "President of Tongde College" should be "Graduate of Tongde College." Please correct this. I would be most grateful. Sincerely, Hu Ding'an, September 24.

To the Editor:

I am writing to you regarding the report in your newspaper on September 25 about the corpse case at the Hongpin Women's Hospital, which stated that Zhang Wenhua had studied at McTyeire School. After checking our school's student rosters for all years, there is no one named Zhang Wenhua. It must be a false rumor and should be corrected. Sincerely, McTyeire School, September 25, 1936.

Sports News

Xu Chengyi Gains Right to Quarterfinals in Paris International Tennis Tournament; Defeats French Davis Cup Doubles Player Bernard; Achieves Successive Victories in Various European Countries; Has Already Become a World-Class Player

Havas News Agency, Paris, September 24: In the quarterfinals of the men's singles of the International Tennis Championships organized by the French Jockey Club, Chinese Davis Cup player Xu Chengyi won again, defeating French Davis Cup doubles player Bernard. The score was 2-6, 6-2, 7-5. Xu has achieved successive victories in various European countries and has already become a world-class tennis player. At the beginning of today's match, Bernard won several consecutive games and easily won the first set with 6-2. At the beginning of the second set, the situation immediately changed. Xu launched a fierce attack, forcing Bernard to adopt a defensive posture without the ability to counterattack. Xu then won the second set 6-2. After the break, they fought again. Xu took the lead 2-1 from the start, and Bernard immediately counterattacked, making it 2-2. After that, Xu launched a fierce attack, and Bernard also tried his best to resist, so the situation in this set was extremely tense. The competition between the two sides was very fierce, with victories seen on both sides, but in the end, Xu defeated Bernard 7-5 and qualified for the semifinals.

Women's 400-Meter Freestyle Final

The women's 400-meter freestyle final was held at 3:50 PM. The championship was contested by Mastenbroek of the Netherlands and Hove of Denmark. Both broke the previous大会 record of 5 minutes 28.5 seconds set by Taddison of the United States in the last tournament.

(Men's 1500-Meter Freestyle Final)

At 4:10 PM, the men's 1500-meter freestyle final was a magnificent spectacle. All three Japanese participants qualified for the final. Although the United States also had two participants, only Mediga could compete with them. Although the Japanese athlete Terada Noboru did not achieve excellent results in the semifinals, his strength was generally recognized. After the start, Mediga competed fiercely with him, not showing any weakness. After 1000 meters, the superior and inferior situation was already clear. Terada Noboru encouraged himself to move forward, and Mediga gradually became unsustainable. Another Japanese athlete, Azuma Shohei, caught up from behind and fought a fierce battle with Mediga for second place. As a result, Terada Noboru reached the finish line first, 28 meters ahead. Mediga defeated Azuma Shohei by half a meter, but the result was not as good as the大会 record (19 minutes 12.4 seconds set by Kitamura Kusuo of Japan in the previous大会).

Finnish Hakator Creates New World Record for Two Miles: 8 Minutes 57.4 Seconds

Havas News Agency, Stockholm, September 24: At the two-mile race held here, Finnish athlete Hakator (the champion of the 11th Olympic Games 9,000-meter race and who recently set a world record of 8 minutes 14.8 seconds in the 3,000-meter race here) won again, breaking the world record for the two-mile race with a time of 8 minutes 57.4 seconds. Strong Buying by Major Financial Players Keeps Gold Prices Firm

The gold market continued its upward trend yesterday. It opened steadily, and although it briefly weakened due to short-selling activities, strong buying by major players ultimately kept prices firm. Initially, overseas silver markets were flat in both London and New York. It was said that after the market closed, the major players had not satisfied their buying orders at the listed prices, while sellers remained inactive. Speculation suggested that Mondelez's forward silver price would either remain unchanged or rise by seven points. Exchange rates generally declined. London spot gold rose by half a penny. The Central Bank's bid price was announced, with both London and New York remaining flat, and the Customs Gold Unit unchanged. The standard gold price was listed at $1116.10. Pre-market trading opened at $26.50. Chafeng, Yongding, and Kang bought heavily, pushing prices to over $7. Dachengsheng took advantage of the high prices to offer gold, causing prices to fall back to $6.78. The morning opening was still high. After the opening, major players sold off heavily, and spot market participants also sold, causing a gradual decline. Buyers took advantage of the low prices to maintain the market. The HSBC's listed prices were announced, with both London and New York remaining flat, causing prices to rise again. The Silver Equalization Tax was announced as unchanged, causing the market to stabilize. Major players continued to supply gold. Although there were rumors of a further decline, buyers flocked in at $5.78, leading to stability. In the afternoon market, prices opened steadily due to strong buyer demand and gradually rose, turning the market bullish. Reports of long positions by Indian silver speculators in Anna and others led to short-selling at high prices and a pullback. Ultimately, the supply side was calmer, and the one-time Indian silver price was also flat, leading to market consolidation. Forward rates were posted by long positions at $3 yesterday. Here is a record of the day's market conditions:

The morning opening was at $1126.70, up half a dollar from the previous close. Chafeng, Yongda, Dachengsheng, Fuyu, Tongfengheng, and others sold, pushing prices down to $5.30. Chafengyong took advantage of the low prices to buy, pushing prices up to $6.70. The closing price was $1126.50.

Although Buying Sentiment is Weak, Cotton Ultimately Drives the Yarn Market

The cotton market is quite firm due to brisk yarn sales and naturally strong factory demand. Prices from various producing areas have not loosened, and sources have not been eager. Currently, short sellers are using old, coarse cotton to put pressure on the market, and as new cotton comes to market, buyers are not as numerous as in the cotton yarn market. Moreover, some are buying yarn and selling cotton, engaging in arbitrage.

Piece Goods: Increased Costs Make Cotton Cloth More Profitable

Yesterday, marked yarn prices suddenly surged, and spot yarn became increasingly profitable. Various weaving factories saw strong demand for cotton cloth. Shortages of yarn have made spot goods increasingly firm and expensive. The sudden increase in the cost of cotton cloth is also generally seen as favorable. White goods merchants are aggressively raising the price of fine cloth and fine twill, by five cents to one dime per piece. Fine cloth, fine twill, and coarse cloth from local factories have also risen by about one dime, and they are all struggling to supply enough goods. Yesterday, dyeing factories in the city purchased more than 300 pieces of fine cloth and fine twill of Japanese origin. Merchants from this street, Ningbo, Shaoxing, and Hankou purchased more than 400 pieces of coarse cloth, fine cloth, and fine twill from factories such as Yih Ho, Da Sheng, Zhen Tai, and Shen Zha. Factories have raised the prices of printed goods, minimum grade gabardine, line tweed, and other goods particularly sharply, by about one or two dimes. However, most factories still need time to deliver on existing orders and are urgently seeking to reduce orders. They are unwilling to accept high-priced spot transactions. The market is exceptionally firm and expensive, and demand from all quarters is particularly keen, it is said.

Felt Boot Cloth Demand has Started

The current sales of felt boot cloth are quite brisk, and market prices are firm. Since the Chongqing-Chengdu merchant groups have been actively purchasing, the inventory in Shanghai has decreased. New goods arriving in Shanghai are very scarce, and costs also need to be increased by about 10%. Currently, merchants from Tianjin are also showing great interest in purchasing. Shoe stores on this street with relatively ample funds are also preparing to purchase. However, the stock of goods is lacking, and there are many incomplete patterns and colors, causing buyers considerable disappointment.

Food: Short Squeeze This Month, Flour Prices Rise Consistently in Near and Deferred Months

Yesterday morning, at the opening of the flour market, prices for all months rose. This was because quotations for foreign wheat were up 8.0 cents near-month and 4-5 cents deferred-month in Chicago, and about 5 cents in Canada. At the opening, because this month's contracts were nearing settlement, with the exchange setting the 26th as the final date, general short sellers and some small factories rushed to cover their positions, causing the market to steadily rise. For deferred months, outside speculators also began to absorb contracts, causing the market atmosphere to gradually tighten, up 2-3 cents from the previous day. At the afternoon opening, this month's contracts rose by 2 cents at the start, and afterwards, few sellers emerged. Short sellers scrambled to cover, leading to a short squeeze, and prices finally rose to 3.2625 yuan. Deferred-month contracts remained strong because of the tightness in near-month contracts, even though factories modestly sold short. As a result, prices rose by 4-6 cents across the board. These prices were recent record highs. Looking ahead, market sentiment this month may lead to further turbulence, it is feared.

The joint company held its fourth weekly auction of Guangdong accumulated sugar yesterday. The total amount set was more than 7,000 bags, at 11.4 yuan. Quxi Factory also offered 125 bags at 21 yuan. The municipal new factory also offered 100 bags at 21.2 yuan, and 50 bags of medium-grained white sugar at 19.3 yuan. A total of 920 bags were traded.

Silk and Tea: Shanghai Silk Rises Continuously, but Yesterday Prices Began to Soften

Yesterday, overseas silk markets showed mixed gains and losses. Raw silk trading on the New York Stock Exchange was again lackluster. Near-term contracts were up 1.5 cents from the previous period, while deferred contracts were down 1 cent. Yokohama was down 5-10 yuan. The Lyons silk market remained sluggish. The Shanghai silk market seemed to have reached its peak and prices softened. The silk exchange remained quiet. Foreign firms such as Jardine Matheson and Wing On slightly increased purchases, and there were also sporadic purchases of Qilihui, Jing Shuanggong, and other silk varieties. The end-user silk market showed a slight increase in buying interest, and silk prices also softened. For example, Zebra grade silk, which previously held a price of 680 yuan, fell by about 5 yuan yesterday, with sell orders at 675 or 672.50 yuan. It is hoped that sales will be achieved at that price. The remaining ordinary B-grade silk generally fell by 3-5 yuan or 2.5 yuan. Yesterday, the total volume of domestic and foreign silk sales in the city was 106 bales.

Qimen Black Tea is in Short Supply and Prices Rise, Green Tea Sales Show Some Activity

After British firms such as Jardine Matheson and Hsieh Ho absorbed large quantities of Qimen black tea in previous days, yesterday the China Tea Trading Corporation, Wang Yutai, Hsieh Ho, and other firms continued to purchase 1,800-1,900 boxes. Due to the shortage of goods, market prices rose by 5-6 yuan compared to the previous day. The market currently has only 700-800 boxes remaining. The entire sales plan can be said to be fully realized at this point. The green tea market has also shown some activity in the past two days. Hsieh Ho, Yi He, Tongfu, and other firms have all purchased Lulianzhuang Zhenmei and Needle tea. However, because import prices from Morocco are tight, market prices still show no sign of rising.

According to a report from the Tea Association, the tea market has been more active recently. In particular, Ping-Shui eyebrow tea sales have been quite brisk since the market price was equalized. It is reported that Jardine Matheson, Hsieh Ho, China Tea, and Yih Ho all made substantial purchases, with high-grade teas selling for 22-25 yuan, medium-grade teas selling for 15-17 yuan, and lower-grade teas selling for 13-14 yuan, totaling more than 5,700 boxes. In addition, Yih Ho purchased 1,500 boxes of green Tong shrimp eye tea at a price of 53 yuan. Tongfu purchased 500 small boxes of Dagang tea, mainly from Yih Ho, with most of them being Embroidery eyebrow tea priced at approximately 15-16 yuan. Other companies such as Zhen Xie He Tianxiang also traded a few dozen to a hundred boxes each, and Zhen Mei Yi He Baolong also had their own respective purchase agents. It is observed that the prices of all teas sold were stable.

Hardware: Prime Virgin Lead Prices Rise Sharply, Overseas Demand Increases Significantly, Affecting the Local Market

Prime virgin lead trading has been quiet for a long time because prices were too high, and most buyers switched to purchasing native lead and recycled lead, with little interest in foreign lead. However, since yesterday and the day before, market trends have changed dramatically. Overseas news indicates that due to the Spanish war, lead is an essential item for manufacturing military equipment, so all countries are competing to buy it, and the market price has soared by one pound, with each ton selling for eighteen pounds, with few spot goods available. Local firms, upon receiving this news, are hoarding goods. The market has a shortage of supply and strong demand, and prices have jumped 1.5 yuan, with each dan selling for 25 yuan. Native lead is also selling for 23 yuan, and recycled lead is 21-22 yuan, with prices firm across the board. 200-300 pieces were traded, with most of the sales being made to merchants from the Rong district. Local families have only inquired and have not yet placed orders.

Oil Market: New Tung Oil Production Period is Approaching

Since the sharp drop in tung oil prices, markets in various places have become depressed. Although 洋荘 [yáng zhuāng] (foreign firms) in Hankou have sporadic transactions, there are no large transactions, resulting in very little market vitality and stagnant inventories. As the saying goes, "Expensive goods remain unsold." However, with 洋荘 [yáng zhuāng] (foreign firms) wanting to purchase spot goods, 行家 [háng jiā] (industry experts) are not willing to sell them cheaply, so transactions still require a foreign standard price of 53-54 yuan per dan. It is heard that new oil has been offered for sale from November to January of the new year, with prices ranging from 47 yuan to 48 yuan, and several hundred tons have been traded. Later, the price will need to be 50 yuan. For 洋行 [yáng háng] (foreign firms), they have a stronger interest in 期油 [qí yóu] (futures oil) and are focusing on futures. The few spot goods they take are priced casually and taken at will, so all merchants do not pay much attention to the spot oil market in Hankou, mainly to observe the overall market situation. In Zhejiang, new production starts earlier, and new goods are expected to arrive in Shanghai in late October. Therefore, merchants from Hangzhou have been offering 3,000-4,000 砠 [zhǔ] of oil in Shanghai every day, with the highest price being 46 yuan per 砠 [zhǔ] (a small number), but the vast majority were at the lowest price of 40 yuan. It is heard that spot goods still need 52-53 yuan delivered to Shanghai. However, this year, local tung oil firms in Shanghai have jointly agreed to refuse the practice of 洋貨 [yáng huò] (foreign goods) before 本貨 [běn huò] (domestic goods), so all transactions are for 洋貨 [yáng huò] (foreign goods) and 本貨 [běn huò] (domestic goods) to be delivered simultaneously. This is also because in previous years, merchants suffered losses from selling goods before delivering them, as they had delivery deadlines, and if the seller defaulted, they would have to make separate arrangements to deliver and bear the losses. Therefore, there is a joint effort to ban this practice. Furthermore, the 洋鐵箱 [yáng tiě xiāng] (foreign iron boxes) used to store tung oil have also been uniformly changed to standard boxes, so the long-standing problem of heavy boxes has been eliminated, the box issue has been clarified, and the tung oil industry will benefit greatly.

Statistics: The Economic Research Department of the Central Bank Releases Production Index for June

The production index compiled by the Economic Research Department of the Central Bank, previously published in major daily newspapers and the Bank's monthly report prior to May of this year, is now known to have been calculated for June as 105.7, higher than any other month this year, which is a good sign for the future of the industry.
